2a1(mdo sde): bya// a b+hi ni ska ma na sU tra/
2a2(mdo sde): a b+hi ni sgra ma na sU tra/
2a3(mdo sde): bod skad du/ mngon par 'byung ba'i mdo// dkon
2a4(mdo sde): mchog gsum la phyag 'tshal lo// gang zhig
2b1(mdo sde): nyid kyi dbu ni rin chen 'od ldan dang / btsun mo pad ma kha bye mi rnyed
2b2(mdo sde): mdangs ldan pas/ slong ba dga' mdzad sangs rgyas go 'phang brnyes
2b3(mdo sde): gyur cing / chos rnams ston mdzad zhi ba de la phyag 'tshalo// gang zhig
2b4(mdo sde): rnyed pas ngan 'gro'i 'jigs las 'das gyur cing / srid pa'i
3a1(mdo sde): 'ching ba thams cad zad byed zhir 'gyur la/
3a2(mdo sde): sdug bsngal mtha' me la ba'i rnam la dag
3a3(mdo sde): ba'i/ zam pa gcig pu bde gshegs chos la
3b1(mdo sde): 'tshal lo// gang la yon tan phul byung la gnas sbyin pa'i
3b2(mdo sde): gnas// mchod pa cung zad byas kyi'i rgya cid 'gyur ba/
3b3(mdo sde): bde bar gshegs pas rab bsngags gang zag mchog brgyad
3b4(mdo sde): kyis// rab brgyan 'phags pa'i dge 'dun de la phyag 'tshalo//
4a1(mdo sde): thub gsung rnam par bltas na dad pa mi bskyed pa
4a2(mdo sde): 'am/ phan pa mi 'byung gang de ci yang yod min la// tshig tu ba dang 'dzin
4a3(mdo sde): pa'i nus dang rnam bral ba// rnam par g.yengs phyir 'bras stsol 'di
4a4(mdo sde): bdag nyung zad cing // ji ltar pad ma kha bye'i dbus na bung ba ni// 'khor
4b1(mdo sde): zhing pad ma las ni chung zad stsogs par byed// de bzhin thub pa'i zhal gyi pad ma'i tshal nang nas//
4b2(mdo sde): rang yid rab tu dga' byed cung zad sdu bar bya// thub pa'i gsung ni ma lus shin tu rtogs dka'
4b3(mdo sde): ba// dad ldan mi la nyin re'ang rgyas par nye 'gro ste// rnam par dpyad na tshigs bcad phyed mtha'
4b4(mdo sde): 'ang mi dpogs na// rin chen mdo brgya sdu ba 'di ni smos ci dgos// phyogs sgo rnams su
4b5(mdo sde): snyan dang grags pa'i snang bas khyab// rab gsal zhes bya sa'i bdag por gyur pa na//
5a1(mdo sde): bsod nams stobs kyis dgra las rgyal bas rgyal phran gyis// btud
5a2(mdo sde): bas nor bu'i phan 'od kyis zhabs gtsang byas// glang po'i dbang po rgyags 'khrig
5a3(mdo sde): 'dod chags kyis chags pa// 'phral du bcos pa'i thabs med nyon mongs skabs gyur
5a4(mdo sde): la// gzigs nas 'gro ba'i chags stsogs nyes pa zhi bzhed pas// thugs bstan
5a5(mdo sde): thub dbang gyur par de ni smon lam btab/ de nas brtsams te sprin dang tshul khrims bzod
5b1(mdo sde): pa dang // brtson 'grus bsam gtan mig yo blo gros rnon po rnams// nyin bde'i ltos med shin tu yun ring yang
5b2(mdo sde): dag spel// 'gro la phan phyir shin tu dka' ba brgya phrag mdzad// thugs rje che ldan drang srong mchog 'di tshe
5b3(mdo sde): gzhan du// nyid kyis 'gro phan don mdzad mi skyo ji snyed de// brjod par 'di na sha ri'i bus kyang mi nus na'ang /
5b4(mdo sde): ngag dag phyir ni chung zad yongasu brjod par bya// stag mo shi ba'i glang po'i sprin gyi dka' thub dbang // tshangs
5b5(mdo sde): stsogs sku tshe brgya phrag du mar dge mdzad nas// don kun bsgrub brtson bdag nyid chen po che gcig thogs// byang
5b6(mdo sde): chub sems dpas dga' ldan gnas su skye ba zhes// der bzhugs nas ni 'gro ba kun la legs gzigs nas/
6a1(mdo sde): skyabs med g.yo zhing 'ongs pa du mas yongs dab la// thugs rje chen pos thugs ni slob bskyed 'gyur/
6a2(mdo sde): gzhan gyi don mdzad thugs dam nyid kyi rgyud dgongs gyur/ de bas 'di ni ji ltar mi yul nyer gshegs te// skye dang rga shi
6a3(mdo sde): 'jigs pa gzigs nas ni// rab 'byung blo gros nges mdzad byang chub yang dag skyes/ de bzhin chos ston mdzad pa bshad
6a4(mdo sde): kyis mnyan par gyis// de nas dga' ldan gyi gnas na bzhugs pa'i byang chub sems dpa' bskal pa mang por bsod nams
6a5(mdo sde): dang ye shes kyi tshogs dpag tu med pa du mnye bar bsags pas// byang chub kyi phyogs yongasu rdzogs par mdzad pa// nyon
6a6(mdo sde): mongs pa'i chu bo stobs dang ldan pa shin du chod pa rnams la thugs rjes yongs su bskul ba// gzhan gyi don mdzad pa'i phyir
6b1(mdo sde): rtag tu brtson par mdzad pa/ de thugs la dgongs pa 'di lta bu mngon sum du mdzad ga// gang ngas skye ba mang por yongs su
6b2(mdo sde): 'khor ba na// rang gi sha dang khrag dang / mgo dang / mig dang / bu dang / chung ma rnams btang ba dang / shin du btang bas
6b3(mdo sde): yongs su btang ba dang / dka' bas tshul khrims la gnas pa dang / gzhan gyis sbyar ba'i bsnyen bskur ma yin pa sna tshogs pa
6b4(mdo sde): bzod par byas pa dang / rtag tu lhod pa med pa'i spro ba dang / 'bras bu dang / bcas po'i ting nge 'dzin gyi bde ba la ma chags pa dang /
6b5(mdo sde): yod pa med pa'i don la rnam par dpyod pa dang / ldan pas gzhan gyi don la brtson pa'i blo gros gyis// shin tu mi bzad pa'i sdug bsngal
6b6(mdo sde): gyi tshor ba rnam pa mang pos sems la gdungs pa'i sdug 'phongs pa'i srog chags rnams la mchog tu snying rje skyed nas/ byams pa'i stobs
6b7(mdo sde): dang zla 'od dang / shi bi dang / glang po dang thams cad sgrol dang / bzod par smra ba dang / spre'u yi bdag po dang / migs bzangs dang / sman
7a1(mdo sde): smon lam byas shing bsags
7a2(mdo sde): chen po la sogs pa skyes pa'i rab stong phrag sred du/ e ma'o kye ma bdag gis 'jig rten long ba 'dren pa med pa/ yongs
7a3(mdo sde): 'don pa ma da / yongs su 'dren pa med pa/ chos ma yin pa/ 'dod chags kyi dbang du 'gro ba log pa'i chos kyis yongasasu khyab pa/ sems
7a4(mdo sde): la ma bzad pa'i chags pas zil gyis non pa/ khro ba mang ba/ lta ba ngan pa'i tshang tshing gis rnam par rlag pa dang / phra dog dang /
7a5(mdo sde): ser snas kun du 'chings pa/ legs par spod pa la 'jug pa la rgyab kyis phyogs shing nyes par spyod pa la kun du gzhol bar gyur pa rnams la/
7a6(mdo sde): bdag sangs rgyas su gyur nas/ sems can ma dgrol ba rnams ni bsgral bar bya'o// ma grol ba rnams ni grol bar bya'o// dbugs ma phyin pa
7a7(mdo sde): rnams ni dbugs dbyungs par bya'o// yongs su mya ngan las ma 'das pa rnams ni yongs su mya ngan las zla bar bya'o// zhes ngas yun ring /
7a8(mdo sde): du mngon par 'dod pa yin na/ de ni don de bya ba'i dus la bab pa yin gyis/ ma la bdag gis 'jig rten gyis gnas skabs ci zhig yin pa ltas na/
7b1(mdo sde): gdul bar nus so// gdul bar nus so// zhes de ltar rnam par dgongs nas/ 'jig rten 'di dag thams cad la gzigs pa 'jug
7b2(mdo sde): ste/ su ni 'grib/ su ni dge chos rnams kyis 'phel/ su ni gnod par gyur/ su ni nyams thag par gyur/ su ni sdug bsngal bar
7b3(mdo sde): gyur/ gang la ni ngas ma 'jigs shig/ ma 'jigs shig ces mi 'jigs pa sbyin pas dbugs dbyung bar bya'o// su ni ngan song la gzhol/
7b4(mdo sde): su ni ngan song la 'bab/ su ni ngan song las bton te/ mtho ras dang thar pa'i 'bras bu la gzhag par bya/ su ni 'dod pa'i 'dam na bying ba la lag
7b5(mdo sde): nas dran par bya/ su ni 'phags pa'i nor dang bral pa rnams la 'phags pa'i nor gyi dbang phyug gi bdag po la bzhag par bya/ gang gis dge
7b6(mdo sde): ba'i rtsa ba ma bskyed pa dag ni bskyed par bya/ gang gi dge ba'i rtsa ba ma bskyed pa dag ni yongs su smin par bya/ gang gis yongs su rmin pa rnams ni rnam
7b7(mdo sde): par grol bar bya/ zhes ye shes kyi gzigs pa 'jug pa mdzad pa na/ srog chags brgya stong dpag tu med pa la la ni/ dge ba'i rtsa ba ma bskyed
7b8(mdo sde): pa bskyed par 'ongs pa dang / la la dge ba'i rtsa ba ma smin pa yongs su smin par nus pa dang / la la dge ba'i rtsa ba yongs su smin pa bde 'gror 'gro
8a1(mdo sde): zu ba la gzhol ba dang // la la 'bras bu dang po thob par gzhol ba dang // la la lan cig phyir 'ong ba'i 'bras bu dang // phyir
8a2(mdo sde): mi 'ong ba dang // dgra bcom pa nyid dang // rang byang chub 'thob par gzhol ba dang // la la bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa byang chub pa'i bskal pa
8a3(mdo sde): dang ldan pa dang // la la ni sngon gyi smon lam rnams nye bar bsags pas rkyen las rag las pa gang zhig ma thogs pas dam pa'i chos las yongs su nyams par
8a4(mdo sde): gyur pa gzigs so// gzigs nas kyang 'di snyam du dgongs te// kye ma'o bdag gi yun ring po nas yang dag par rtog pa rdzogs par gyur cig/ nga'i
8a5(mdo sde): ngal ba 'bras bu dang bcas par gyur to// zhes dges shing // ngas bya ba dang ni byas so// ngas khur bskur ba rga ba ni/ mthar phyin te// gang nga'i yongs su dag
8a6(mdo sde): pa'i rgyud dang ldan pa'i zhing du gyur cing 'dul bya'i skye'o rnams yun ring por mi thogs par pad ma'i tshal yongs su smin cing kha bye la ma reg pa'i nyi ma shar bas rgyas par 'gyur
8a7(mdo sde): ba lta bur gyur gyis phyi shol mi bya'o// // 'dir gnas bzhin du yang thams cad rdzogs par bya bar nus pa ma yin pas na/ bzhes pa'i dus ni ma yin gyis/
8a8(mdo sde): ma la bdag mi'i 'jig rten du song la der phyin nas brtson 'grus kyi grogs dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i bla na med pa'i ye shes rtogs par bya ste/ 'di
8b1(mdo sde): rnams bskal pa ji lta ba bzhin du 'di rnams kyi dge ba'i rtsa ba bskyed cing yongs su smin la rnam par grol ba bya zhing / skye ba dang / rga ba dang / na ba dang / 'di
8b2(mdo sde): ba dang / mya ngan dang / sme ba sdug 'don pa dang / sdug bsngal ba dang / yid mi bde ba'i sdug bsngal gyi rgya mtshor lhung ba/ skyabs med pa/ yongs su skyob pa
8b3(mdo sde): med pa srog chags rnams// dam pa'i chos bstan pa'i lag pa brkyang pas/ gnod par bya'o// thog ma med pa'i dus nas rjes su 'brel ba'i 'dod chags
8b4(mdo sde): dang / zhe sdang dang / gti mug gi me kun gdungs pa rnams la// 'phags pa'i lam yan lag brgyad pa'i chu'i rgyun blugs pas sdug bsngal ma lus pa bsal
8b5(mdo sde): bar bya'o// zhes de lta bu'i thugs la dgongs pa nyes pa bskyed rnas/ 'dzam pa'i gling du 'jug pa mdzad pa na/ rigs dang / yul dang dus dang / brgyud dang /
8b6(mdo sde): bud med ste// gzigs pa rnams pa lngas gzigs par mdzad do// byang chub sems dpa' rnams rgyu gang gis rigs la gzigs par mdzad ce na/ byang chub sem
8b7(mdo sde): dpa' dga' ldan gyi gnas na/ bzhugs pa ni 'di snyam dgongs te/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams rigs ji lta zhig tu nying mtshams sbyor ba len snyam na/ bram ze'i
8b8(mdo sde): rigs sam/ rgyal rigs su yin na/ de la res 'ga' ni bram ze'i rigs btsun par bkur/ res 'ga' rgyal rigs te/ da lta ni rgyal rigs btsun par bskur bar
9a1(mdo sde): mngon 'asrung / gzigs nas/ ma la bdag la gzhan dag byang chub sems dpa' rigs ngan par nying mtshams sbyor ba slangaso// zhes bzhi 'dis kha zer
9a2(mdo sde): bar mi 'gyur/ bdag gis rgyal rigs su nying mtshams spor ba blang bar bya'o snyam mo// 'di ltar byang chub sems dpa' thogs ma med pa'i dus nas smad par mi 'gyur/
9a3(mdo sde): ba'i las byas shing bsags pa dang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos bshad pa 'bras bu med pa yin pas/ rgyu 'dis ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams
9a4(mdo sde): rigs la gzigs par mdzad do// byang chub sems dpa' rnams rgyu gang gis yul la gzigs par mdzad ce na/ byang chub sems dpa' dga' ldan gyi gnas na bzhag
9a5(mdo sde): pa ni 'di snyam du dgongs te/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams yul ji lta ba zhig tu nying mtshams sbyor ba len snyam na/ 'bras dang / bu ram shing dang / ba lang
9a6(mdo sde): dang / ma he phun sum tshogs pa/ slongs mo pa brgya 'du ba mtha' khob kyi skye bo med pa dbus pa'i skye bo gnas pa gang du skye bo gcig btul bas/ skye bo'i tshogs
9a7(mdo sde): chen po 'dul bar 'gyur ba'i yul gang yin par gzigs so// de nas byang chub sems dpa' 'di snyam du dgongs te/ dbus kyi yul 'di ni bu ram shing gi phreng dang /
9a8(mdo sde): 'bras dang / ba lang dang / ma he phun sum tshogs pa// slongs mo pa brgya 'du ba// mtha' khob kyi skye bo med pa/ dbus pa'i skye bo'i gnas pa gang du skye bo gcig
9b1(mdo sde): btul bas skye bo'i chen po btul bar 'gyur ba yin gyis/ ma la bdag la gzhan dag byang chub sems dpas yul mtha' kho ba rnams su nying mtshams/
9b2(mdo sde): sbyor ba blangs so zhes zer ba 'dis kha zer bar mi 'gyur bar bdag gis yul dbus su nying mtshams sbyor ba blang bar bya'o snyam mo// 'di ltar byang chub
9b3(mdo sde): sems dpa' thogs ma med pa'i dus nas/ smad par mi 'gyur ba'i las byas shing bsags pa dang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos bshad pa
9b4(mdo sde): 'bras bu med pa ma yin pas rgyu 'di ni/ byang chub sems dpa' yul la gzigs pa mdzad do// byang chub sems dpa' rnams rgyu gang gis na/ dus la gzigs par
9b5(mdo sde): mdzad ce na/ byang chub sems dpa' dga' ldan gyi gnas na bzhugs pa ni 'di snyam du dgongs te/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams dus ji lta ba zhig tu mdzam bu'i gling du nyid
9b6(mdo sde): mtshams sbyor ba len snyam na/ skye dgu'i tshe lo yar skye ba na/ brgyad khri thub pa yan chad nying mtshams sbyor ba mi len la/ mi rnams kyi tshe lo mar 'grib brgya thub pa man
9b7(mdo sde): chad nying mtshams sbyor ba mi len no// byang chub sems dpa' rgyu gang gis rnams kyi tshe lo brgyad khri thub thub pa yan chad nying mtshams sbyor ba len par mi mdzad ce na/
9b8(mdo sde): mi rnams kyi tshe lo brgyad khri thub na/ yid 'byung bar rga zhing skyo bar bya ba dka' la/ blun zhing dbang po brtul ba dang / bag med cing bde ba mang bas/ bden pa rnams
10a1(mdo sde): ra lung #kyi snod du mi 'gyur ba'i phyir ro// mar 'grib pa lo brgya man chad du yang snyigs ma lnga po 'di lta ste/ tshe'i snyigs ma dang / nyon mongs pa'i
10a2(mdo sde): snyigs ma dang / sems can gyi snyigs ma dang / lta ba'i snyigs ma dang / dus kyi snyig ma shas che ba yin pas bdag la gzhan dag byang chub sems dpas snyig ma
10a3(mdo sde): lnga shas che ba'i dus su nying mtshams sbyor ba blangs so zhes gzhi 'dis kha zer bar mi 'gyur ro// 'di ltar byang chub sems dpas thog ma med pa'i dus nas/ smang
10a4(mdo sde): par mi 'gyur ba'i las byas shing brtsigs pa dang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos bshad pa 'bras bu med pa ma yin pas/ rgyu 'dis ni byang chub
10a5(mdo sde): sems dpa' rnams dus la gzigs pa yin no// byang chub sems dpa' rnams rgyu gang gis rgyu la gzigs par mdzad ces na/ byang chub sems dpa' dga'
10a6(mdo sde): ldan gyi gnas na bzhugs pa ni 'di snyam du dgongs te/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams rgyud ci 'dra ba zhig tu nying mtshams sbyor ba len snyam na/ rigs gang zhig btsan
10a7(mdo sde): par bkur zhing ma myes zung bdun pa myes gyi bar spyod pa la skyon med par gzigs nas/ de sgom du dgongs te/ shAkya'i rigs rgyud 'di ni btsun par bkur ba
10a8(mdo sde): yin zhing mang pos bkur ba nas bzung ba ste/ spyod pa skyon med pa yin gyis ma la bdag la gzhan dag byang chub sems dpas rgyud ngan pa las nying mtshams
10b1(mdo sde): sbyor ba blangs so zhes gzhi 'dis kha zer bar mi 'gyur bar/ bdag gi rgyal po zas gtsang ma rgyud du nying mtshams sbyor ba blang ngo snyam mo// 'di ltar byang chub sems
10b2(mdo sde): thog ma med pa'i dus nas sman par mi 'gyur ba'i las byas shing bsags pa dang // sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos bshad pa 'bras bu med pa ma yin pa//
10b3(mdo sde): rgyu 'di na byang chub sems dpa' rgyud la gzigs par mdzad do// byang chub sems dpa' rnams rgyu gang gis bud med la gzigs par mdzad ce na/ byang chub
10b4(mdo sde): sems dpa' dga' ldan gyi gnas na bzhugs pa ni 'di snyam du dgongs te/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams bud med ci 'dra ba zhig gis rum du nying mtshams sbyor ba
10b5(mdo sde): len snyam na/ de 'di snyam du dgongs te/ bud med gang zhig gzugs bzang mo dang ldan pa/ rigs dang ldan pa/ rigs 'phel bar 'gyur ba/ khro bag
10b6(mdo sde): can ma yin pa/ phra ma can ma yin pa/ ngag rtsub pa ma yin pa/ dad pa dang ldan pa dang / rang bzhin bzang ba/ bsam pa dge ba/ rgyud phun sum tshogs pa/
10b7(mdo sde): rigs mtho ba// nye du'i rigs dang ldan pa// shes rab phun sum tshogs pa// gtong ba phun sum tshogs pa// mtshan nyid mi g.yo ba/ rang bzhin brtan la rgod
10b8(mdo sde): bag can ma yin pa/ khengs pa med pa/ byams pa'i sems dang ldan pa/ sdug cing yid du 'ong ba/ 'jig rten thams cad la chos dang ldan pa/ bud med thams cad kyi
11a1(mdo sde): mang 'byung / @mchog tu gyur pa// sangs rgyas rnams la/ e ma'o bdag sangs rgyas kyi yum du gyur cig ces smon lam btab pa dang / byang chub sems
11a2(mdo sde): dpa' zla ba bcu rum du 'dzin nus pa dang / rang gi don du yang nyams par mi byed pa yin par gzigs so// de nas byang chub sems dpa' 'di snyam du dgongs te/ sgyu
11a3(mdo sde): 'phrul chen mo 'di ni ma myes dang pha myes zung bdun gyi bar du spod pa la skyon med cing gzugs dang ldan pa dang / rig dang ldan pa dang / tshul dang ldan zhes bya ba nas/ bud
11a4(mdo sde): med thams cad kyi mchog tu gyur ces bya ba'i bar gong ma bzhin te/ khro bag can ma yin pa dang / rigs 'phel bar 'gyur ba dang / byang chub sems dpa' rum du zla ba bcur
11a5(mdo sde): 'dzin nus pa dang / rang gi don yang mi nyams pa yin la/ 'di ltar sgyu 'phrul chen mos sngon sangs rgyas rnams la kye ma bdag sangs rgyas kyi yum du gyur cig ces smon lam
11a6(mdo sde): btab pa yang yin pas/ bdag la gzhan dag byang chub sems dpa' mtshan ngan pa dang / ldan pa'i bud med kyi tsam du nying mtshams sbyor ba blangs so zhes kha zer bar mi
11a7(mdo sde): 'gyur ro// snyam mo 'di ltar byang chub sems dpas sman par mi 'gyur ba'i las byas shing bsags pa dang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnam ni chos bshad pa 'bras bu med
11a8(mdo sde): ba ma yin pas/ rgyu 'dis na byang chub dpa' bud med rnams la gzigs par mdzad do// de nas byang chub sems dpa' gzigs pa lngas gzigs nas
11b1(mdo sde): dga' ldan na spyod pa'i lha'i rigs rnams la gsungs pa/ grogs po dag shes par gyis shig/ nga 'dzam bu'i gling du babs nas yul dbus su nying mtshams
11b2(mdo sde): sbyor ba len gyis khyed cag las gang dag bdud rtsi don du gnyer ba de phal cher yul dbus kyi grong khyer chen po drug po 'di lta ste/ mnyan yod dang / sa ge
11b3(mdo sde): ta dang / yangs pa can dang / tsam pa dang / rgyal po'i khab dang / ba ra na ser nying mtshams sbyor bar long shig/ de skad ces bka' stsal pa dang / dga'
11b4(mdo sde): ldan gyi rig kyi lha rnams kyis byang chub sems dpa' la 'di skad ces gsol to// byang chub sems dpa' mkhyen par mdzod cig/ da ltar 'jig rten ni sdig
11b5(mdo sde): pas gos pa dang / skye dgu ni ma rungs pa'i bsam pa can/ 'dzam bu'i gling ni rtog ge drug dang / rjes su sgrogs pa drug dang / snyoms par 'jug pa drug gis
11b6(mdo sde): bkrugs pa lag so// de la rtog ge drug gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste 'od bsrung rdzogs byed dang / kun du rgyu gnag lhas kyi bu dang / smang 'dod kyi bu me'i bu yang dag rgyal ba
11b7(mdo sde): can dang / mi 'pham smra'i la ba can dang / ka' t+ya'i bu nog can dang / gcer bu pa gnyen gyi bu'o// rjesu sgrog pa drug gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste bram ze rgyus rgyal dang / bram ze rnam rdeg dang /
11b8(mdo sde): bram ze bzang ldan dang / bram ze tshang ba'i tshe dang / bram ze tshad ma'i snying po dang / bram ze mar po'o// snyoms par 'jug pa gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ rig byed kyi bu lhag spyod dang /
11'a1(mdo sde): rgyu rtsal shes kyi bu ring pur dang / kun du rgyu rab bzang dang / bram ze'i khye'u kun rgyal dang / drang srong nyon mongs med dang / lteng rgyas 'od
11'a2(mdo sde): bsrungs ra lA can no// 'dir ni chos nyan pa'i slad du/ byang chub sems dpo' khyed kyi gdan dpag tshad bcu gnyis bsham pa bgyi zhing / bdag cag 'di snyam du bdag cag
11'a3(mdo sde): la dga' ldan gyi gnas na byang chub sems dpa' bzhugs pas chos bshad de/ chos de bdag cag gis thos nas ci nas kyang bdag cag gis yun ring po'i don dang / sman pa dang /
11'a4(mdo sde): bde bar 'gyur ba de lta de ltar bsgrub par bgyid par sems legs so// de skad ces gsol pa dang / byang chub sems dga' ldan gyi lha rnams la 'di skad gsungs so// /
11'a5(mdo sde): grogs po dag de'i phyir rol me'i cha byed thams cad brdungs shig/ dga' ldan gyi ris kyi lha rnams kyis rol mo'i cha byad thams cad brdungs pa dang / byang chub sems
11'a6(mdo sde): dpas kyang dung bus te gsungs pa/ grogs po dag 'di lhag par sgra gang che/ bcom ldan 'das dung gi sgra lags so// grogs po dag ji ltar dung gi sgras rol mo'o
11'a7(mdo sde): cha byad thams cad zil gyis gnan te/ gnas pa de bzhin dungs kyang 'dzam bu'i gling du song la/ rtog ge drug pa dang rjes su sgrogs pa drug dang / snyoms par 'jug
11'a8(mdo sde): pa drug zil gyis gnan nas/ bdud rtsi rtogs par bya ste/ bdud rtsis 'gro ba tshim par bya'o// mi rtag pa'i dung 'bud bar bya'o// stong pa nyid kyi rnga brdungs par bya'o//
11'b1(mdo sde): zhes gsungs nas/ tshigs su bcad de gsungs pa/ seng ge gcig gis gcan zan tshogs ni du ma 'joms/ rdo rje gcig gis brag gi rtse mo du ma 'jig/ brgya
11'b2(mdo sde): byin gcig gis lha ma yin du ma 'joms// nyi ma gcig gis mun pa du ma rnam par sel/ grogs po dag khyed cag las gang bdud rtsi don du gnyer ba de/ yul
11'b3(mdo sde): dbus kyi grong khyer chen po drug tu nying mtshams sbyor ba long shig/ de nas lha rnams kyi dbang po brgya byin 'di snyam du sems te/ byang chub sems dpa' 'di ni
11'b4(mdo sde): btsun mo sgyu 'phrul chen me'i lhums su nying mtshams sbyor ba len par gzhed kyis/ ma la de la bdag gis gzi brjid sgrub par bya/ lhums kyang sbyang bar bya'o snyam
11'b5(mdo sde): nas/ lha rnams kyi dbang po brgya byin btsun mo sgyu 'phrul chen mo la gzi brjid srabs shing lhums kyang gtsang gtsang mar byas so// de nas byang chub sems dpa' dga'
11'b6(mdo sde): ldan gyi gnas na bzhugs pa/ rigs dang / yul dang / dus dang / rgyud dang / bud med la gzigs pa ste/ gzigs pa lngas gzigs pa nas/ nam gyi gung la glang po chen
11'b7(mdo sde): yum gyi lhums su zhugs so// gang gi tshe byang chub sems dpa' dga' ldan gyi lha'i ris nas shi 'phos te/ yum gyi lhums su zhugs pa de'i tshe/ sa chen po 'di
11'b8(mdo sde): shin du g.yos par gyur/ 'jig rten 'di thams cad snang ba chen pos gsal bar gyur cing / 'jig rten 'jig rten gyis par gyi mun pa mun nag skrag tu gyur pa/ gang du
11'b9(mdo sde): dga' ldan gyi lha'i ris nas
12a1(mdo sde): ngo bya/ nyi ma dang zla ba 'di ltar rdzu 'phrul che ba/ 'di mthu che ba dag gis/ 'od kyis snang bar mi nus pa de dag kyang / de'i tshe snang ba chen pos
12a2(mdo sde): gsal bar gyur to// der sems can gang dag skyes pa de dag rang gi lag pa brkyang ba mi mthong ba las/ de rnams snang ba des gcig gis gcig mthong nas shes ldan dang sems
12a3(mdo sde): can gzhan yang 'dir skyes so// shes ldan sems can gzhan yang 'dir skyes so zhes bya bar shes so// ji ltar sprin ni rgya chen legs 'dus pa/ chu mang bsags pa rlung gis
12a4(mdo sde): bskyod pa ltar/ de bzhin blo ldan de ni lhums su 'jug/ ston ka'i sprin rum zla rgyas ji bzhin no// gang tshe rtsal ldan mnyam med nyer gshegs la/ de tshe 'jig rten so so'i
12a5(mdo sde): gling bar na/ mun gyis khebs bsal phyogs kun shin du ni/ bsal snang byug gyur 'di 'dir chos nyid do// gang gi tshe byang chub sems dpa' dga' ldan lha'i ris nas
12a6(mdo sde): 'phos te/ yum gyi lhums su zhugs par mdzad pa de nyid kyi mtshan mo sgyu 'phrul chen mos rmi lam bzhi mthong ste/ glang po che'i phru gu dkar po zhig bdag gi rum g.yas pa
12a7(mdo sde): dral nas zhugs pa dang / steng gi na mkha' la skyil mo krung gis 'chag pa dang / seng ge'i bdan la 'dug nas skye bo'i tshogs chen po la chos ston pa dang / lha dang
12a8(mdo sde): lha ma yin du bcas pa'i 'jig rten bdag la phyag byed pa'o// rgyal po zas gtsang mas btsun mo las de thos pa dang / mtshan mkhan rnams la rmi lam 'di ltar ston/
12b1(mdo sde): pa yin dris pa dang / de rnams kyis smras pa/ lha mkhyen par mdzod cig/ gang btsun mo rmi lam du mthong ba glang po che'i phru gu dkar po zhig bdag gi rum g.yas/
12b2(mdo sde): pa dral nas zhugs pa zhes bya ba ni/ 'khor los sgyur ba'i sras bsdam par 'gyur ro// steng gi nam mkha' la 'chag go// zhes bya ba ni rdzu 'phrul che ba dang /
12b3(mdo sde): mthu che bar 'gyur ro// seng ge'i gdan la bzhugs te chos ston to zhes bya ba ni// de yang seng ge'i bdan la bzhugs te 'khor bzhi la chos ston par 'gyur ro//
12b4(mdo sde): lha dang lha ma yin du bcas pa'i 'jig rten bdag la phyag byed do zhes bya ba nas/ gal te rab tu 'byung bar gyur na/ lha dang lha ma yin du bcas pa'i 'jig rten gyis
12b5(mdo sde): mchod cing brjod la mngon par bstod par 'gyur ro// chos nyid kyis gang gis tshe/ byang chub sems dpa' dga' ldan gyi lha'i ris nas 'phos te yum gyi lhums na
12b6(mdo sde): su zhugs pa de'i tshe/ lha rnams kyi dbang po brgya byin gyis de la mi ma yin pa sus kyang mche bar mi 'gyur bar lha'i bu bzhi yum gyi srangs mar 'jog pa ni/ lag na
12b7(mdo sde): ral gri dang / lag na mdung dang / lag na mdung thung dang / lag na mda'o che'o// de la 'di skad ces bya ste/ lha mchog bzhi la brgya byin gyis
12b8(mdo sde): smras pa/ khyed rnams song la lha mi rnams kyis ni/ shin du mchog gyur yum de ltar su la yang / gnod mi byed par gus pas yongs su bsrung / de rnams
13a1(mdo sde): @#shin du 'bang byas dga' ba dang / brgya byin lung ni skye bos gnan nas su/ rnam kun mdu ral gri lag na thogs/ byang chu
13a2(mdo sde): sems dpa'i yum ni srung bar byed/ g.yul du rgyal gyur lha bzhis sbas pa dang / de ni nyin mtshams sna tshogs rgyan cing zhing / lha mo rang khyim ngan nas rnam grol rol/
13a3(mdo sde): dga' ba'i na spyod pa lta bur spyod/ de nas dus gzhan zhig na/ btsun mo sgyu 'phrul chen mo 'di lta bu'i 'dod pa skyes te/ kye ma'o lha brtson thams cad thar bar bgyi'o//
13a4(mdo sde): rgyal po zas gtsang mas kyang btsun mo'i tshig gnyan nas/ brtson thams cad thar bar byas so// de nas dus gzhan zhig na btsun mo 'dod pa skyes pa/ kye ma'o lhas
13a5(mdo sde): grong khyer gyi shar phyogs kyi dbus su dman pa dang / long ba dang bkren pa dang / sdug 'phongs pa dang / slongs mo pa rnams la sbyin pa byin/ bsod nams dag
13a6(mdo sde): byas pa dang / lho dang nub dang / byang dang / sum mdo dbus su dman pa dang / long ba dang / bkren pa dang / sdug phongs pa dang / spongs mo pa
13a7(mdo sde): rnams la sbyin pa byin bsod nams ni bgyi'o// de nas rgyal po zas gtsang gyis btsun mo'i tshig mnyan nas grong khyer gyi shar phyogs dman pa dang / long ba dang /
13a8(mdo sde): bkren pa dang / sdug phongs pa dang / slongs mo pa rnams la ji ltar mngon par 'dod pa dang / ji ltar spangs pa bzhin du sbyin pa byin bsod nams ni byas pa dang /
13b1(mdo sde): de bzhin du lho dang / nub dang / byang dang / sum mdo'i dbus su dman pa dang / long ba dang / bkren pa dang / sdug phongs pa dang / slongs mo pa rnams
13b2(mdo sde): gang mngon par 'dod pa dang / ji ltar spangs pa bzhin ngas sbyin pa ni byin bsod nams ni byas so// gang gi tshe byang chub sems dpa' shAkya thub pa dga' ldan gyi lha'i ris nas
13b3(mdo sde): 'phos nas/ yum gyi lhums na bzhugs pa dang / mdzod kyi nang du rdzas gzhag pa bzhin du mngal gyi dri ma dang / sha ma'i dri ma dang / khrag gi dri ma dang / mi gtsang
13b4(mdo sde): gang yang rung ba sna tshogs kyis ma sbags so// dper na nor bu rin po che ka sho'i ras kyis mi gro ba dang / ka shi ras kyang nor bu rin po ches mi gos pa de bzhin du/ gang gi
13b5(mdo sde): tshe byang chub sems dpa' yum gyi lhums su bzhugs pa na/ mdzod kyi nang du rdzas gzhag pa bzhi du mngal gyi dri ma dang / sha ma'i dri ma dang / khrag gi dri ma dang /
13b6(mdo sde): mi gtsang ba gang yang rung ba sna tshogs kyis ma spags so// ji ltar nor bu mtshon shel 'od gsal dang / ras gtsang ka sha'i ras kyang gos pa med/ de bzhin thub chen
13b7(mdo sde): lhums na bzhugs pa na/ mngal gyi dri ma cis kyang gos pa med/ gang gis tshe byang chub sems dpa' dga' ldan gyi lha'i rig nas 'phos nas yum gyi lhums na bzhug
13b8(mdo sde): pa de'i tshe/ yum gyi lhums ni de thams cad yongs su rdzogs par bzhugs pa mthong ngo // dper na nor bu bai DUr+ya zur brgyad pa bzang po// rigs dang ldan pa/
14a1(mdo sde): dang ba gsal ba/ dri ma med pa/ tshon skud sna lnga sngon po dang / ser po dang / dmar po dang / dkar po dang / leb
14a2(mdo sde): rgan la rgyus la/ de skyes bu mig dang ldan pas mthong na/ 'di ni skud pa'o// 'di ni nor bu'o// skud pa 'di la nor bu rgyus pa yin no zhes shes pa de bzhin du/ gang gi tshe
14a3(mdo sde): byang chub sems dpa' shAkya thub pa dga' ldan gyi gnas nas 'phos te/ yum gyi lhums na bzhugs de'i tshe/ de'i yum gyi lhums na rnam pa thams cad yongs su rdzogs pa
14a4(mdo sde): lhums kyi nang na bzhugs pa mthong ngo // ji ltar dri med nor bu bai DUr+ya// 'do gsal lag par gzhag pa snang ba ltar/ de bzhin thub chen yum gyi lhums bzhugs pa na/
14a5(mdo sde): shes shing sems pas yum ni yang dag blta/ chos nyid kyis kya dgi tshe byang chub sems dpa' shAkya thub pa dga' ldan nas yum gyi lhums na bzhugs pa de'i tshe/ de'i yum 'di
14a6(mdo sde): lta ste/ byang chub sems dpa' 'dzin pas lus ngal ba 'am lus dub par 'gyur ba med do// las kyi rnam smin zad pas las kyi rnam smin zad pas mtho ris 'phos// gang
14a7(mdo sde): che 'di ni lhums thugs zhugs pa na/ de'i yum ngal bas 'dzin par mi byed par/ de'i tshe gyur pa 'dir de chos nyid do// chos nyid kyis gang gi tshe/ byang chub sems
14a8(mdo sde): dpa' shAkya thub dga' ldan gyi gnas nas 'phos nas/ yum gyi lhums na bzhugs pa de'i tshe/ yum de phan cad ji srid mtsho'i bar brtul zhugs lnga'i bzhi blangs par gyur
14b1(mdo sde): te/ de srid mtsho'i bar du srog spyod pa spangs te/ srog gcod pa las slar ldog go// ma sbyin par len pa dang / mi tshangs par spyod pa dang / brdzun du sla ba
14b2(mdo sde): dang / 'bru'i chang dang / sbyar ba'i chang myos par 'gyur ba bag med pa'i gnas spangs te/ 'bru'i chang dang / sbyar ba'i chang mos par 'gyur ba bag med pa'i gnas
14b3(mdo sde): las slar ldog par byed do// srog mi gcod dang mi byin len pa dang / brdzun mi smra dang tshang la mi brkam dang / 'khrig pa'i mi tshangs spyod pa spong ba 'di/ 'dir ni don grub
14b4(mdo sde): yum gyi chos nyid yin/ chos nyid gang gi tshe/ byang chub sems dpa' shAkya thub pa dga' ldan gyi gnas na 'phos nas/ yum gyi lhums na bzhugs pa de'i yum 'di lta ste/
14b5(mdo sde): skyes pa rnams la 'dod pa dang ldan pa'i yid gtong ba med do// nyon mongs pa rnams la chags par mi 'gyur zhing / de ni 'dod rgyas sems gdung mi 'gyur la/ de yum
14b6(mdo sde): 'dod pa'i yon tan ldan pa'i/ skyes pa rnams la sems ni gtong ba med/ de nas dus gzhan zhig na/ btsun mo sgyu 'phrul chen mo 'dod pa skyes pa skye ma bdag gis
14b7(mdo sde): rgya mtsho chen po bzhi'i chu btung ngo // sum nas des rgyal po zas gtsang la sbas pa dang / rgyal po zas gtsang gis mtshan mkhan rnams la smras pa/ pri'i ci'i
14b8(mdo sde): phyir btsun mo 'di lta bu'i 'dod pa skye/ mtshan mkhan rnams kyis lha btsun mo la sras skyes bu chen po'i mtshan sum bcu rtsa gnyis kyis sku rgyan pa zhig lham par 'gyur te/
15a1(mdo sde): de rab tu byung nas shes bya'i rgya mtsho mtha' dag mthung bar 'gyur ro zhes lung bstan to// rgyal po zas gtsang gis smras pa/ gal te 'di
15a2(mdo sde): la mtsho chen po'i chu ma blud na cir 'gyur/ de rnams kyis smras pa// sras yan lag ma tshang ba zhig btsas par 'gyur ro// rgyal pos smras pa/ nga'i ming zas gtsang
15a3(mdo sde): zhes bya ba'i bu yan lag ma tshang bar bya 'am// de'i grong khyer ser skya'i bzhin kun du rgyu mig dmar zhes bya ba mig 'phrul la byang ba zhig 'dug pa de/ rgyal pos bkug nas/
15a4(mdo sde): rgya mtsho chen po las chu myur bar khug shig ces bsgo ba dang / de de nyid ni 'dug bzhin du rgya mtsho chen po bzhi'i chu drangs te de rnams la btsun mo mthung ngu bcug pa dang / de'i 'dod
15a5(mdo sde): pa skyes pa gang yin pa de dang bral bar gyur te// de nas dus gzhan zhig na btsun mo sgyu 'phrul chen mo tshul 'di lta bu'i 'dod pa skyes te/ kye ma 'o bdag lum bi ni'i tshal du
15a6(mdo sde): zhugs la shing gi rtsar yal ga'i mthar 'dug par bya'o snyam mo// de nas rgyal po zas gtsang mas sgyu 'phrul chen mo tshul de lta bu'i 'dod pa skyes par ris nas/ rin po che/
15a7(mdo sde): sna bzhi las byas pa'i khyogs gshams te/ glang po che'i tshogs dang / rta'i tshogs dang / shing rta'i tshogs dang / dpung bu chung gi tshogs te/ dpung gi tsho gas yan
15a8(mdo sde): lag bzhi pa go bskon nas skye bo'i tshogs chen pos yongs su bskor te/ btsun mo sgyu 'phrul chen mo dang lhan cig tu chas nas lum bi ni'i tshal du phyin to// de nas btsun mo/
15b1(mdo sde): sgyu 'phrul chen mos lum bi ni'i cha la mthong ba na/ sems brtse gcig par gyur pa dang / de khyogs la babs te shing mya ngan me tog yang dag par rgyas pa mthong bas dga' ba dang /
15b2(mdo sde): yid bde ba skyes te der song nas me tog dang 'dab ma'i g.yur gyis dud pa'i yal ga la 'jus te/ bud med rgan pas bskor nas gnas so// de nas lha rnams kyi dbang
15b3(mdo sde): po brgya byin 'di snyam du sems te/ btsun mo sgyu 'phrul chen mos sras bltam par nye bar gnas kyis ma la bdag gis byang chub sems dpa' de dang po ltam pa na blang bar bya'o//
15b4(mdo sde): de nas yang bsams pa btsun mo sgyu 'phrul chen mo 'di ni/ ngo tsha shes pa dang ldan pa yin pas/ bdag gi mdun du lham mi phod kyis thabs shig bshams par bya'o//
15b5(mdo sde): snyam nas/ lha'i dbang po brgya byi ni bud med rgan mo zhig gi cha byad du sprul te des gang gis bud med rgad mo de rnams phyogs bcur 'bros par 'gyur ba de lta bu'i rlung dang char
15b6(mdo sde): drag po zhig sprul nas/ de rnams bros pa dang / bdag nyid ma ma rgan me'i cha byad du mngon par sprul nas/ btsun mo sgyu 'phrul chen me'i mdun du 'dug go// chos
15b7(mdo sde): nyid kyis byang chub sems dpa' ni mkhyen bzhin du yum gyi lhums su 'jug pa dang / mkhyen bzhin du gnas pa dang / mkhyen du 'byung ba yin no// de nas byang
15b8(mdo sde): chub sems dpa' de 'di snyam du dgongs te// gang bdag skyes bu tha ma la ba bzhin du mngal gyi sgo nas/ 'byung ba ni tshul dang mthun pa ma yin gyis ma la
16a1(mdo sde): mang / bdag gis yum gyi sku g.yas pa brtol la ba 'byung bar bya'o zhes/ de nas byang chub sems dpa' yum gyi sku g.yas pa
16a2(mdo sde): brtol te/ 'byung ba dang lha'i dbang po brgya byin gyis lag pa gnyis kyis blangs pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' 'di snyam du dgongs te/ brgya byin 'di bdag gis byang chub
16a3(mdo sde): sems dpa' 'di blangs so zhes dregs pa skye bar 'gyur bar mkhyen nas/ ngo bo nyid kyi rdo rje'i snying po can gyi skur byin gyis rlabs te/ lhums su ni yum 'dzin pas nyon mongs
16a4(mdo sde): par ma gyur cig snyam du dgongs nas yang bar mdzad de bzhugs pa yin no// de nas lha'i dbang po brgya byin gyis 'dzin par ma nus pa dang / 'dar bar gyur to// byang chub
16a5(mdo sde): sems dpas bka' stsal pa/ ko'u shi ka thong thong / de skad ces bka' stsal pa dang / lha'i dbang po brgya sprin gyis byang chub sems da pA sa la gzhag go// gzhag pa
16a6(mdo sde): tsam gyis mod la sus kyang ma bzung bar phyogs bzhir gzigs nas gom pa bdun bdun bor zhing tshig tu yang gsung ba/ ko'u shi ka phyogs 'di gang yin/ byang chub sem
16a7(mdo sde): sems dpa' shar phyogs lags so// byang chub sems dpas bka' stsal pa/ ko'u shi ka sems can thams cad kyi sngon du 'gro bar bya'o// phyogs 'di gang
16a8(mdo sde): yin lho phyogs lags so// 'gro ba thams cad kyi yon gnas su gyur par bya'o// phyogs 'di gang yin/ byang phyogs lags so// srid pa'i rgya mtsho las
16b1(mdo sde): rgal bar bya'o// phyogs 'di gang yin/ nub phyogs lags so// de'i skye ba tha ma ni 'di yin par 'gyur ro// skye mchi mthar byed de ni bltam pa na/
16b2(mdo sde): sa la gom pa bdun ni bzhud nas su/ 'di nga'i skye ba tha mar 'gyur yin zhes/ 'jig rten gsum gyi bla ma cig pus gsungs/ chos nyid kyis byang chub sems
16b3(mdo sde): dpa' shakya thub pa yum gyi lhums nas byung ba de'i tshe/ sa chen po 'di shin du g.yos par gyur/ 'jig rten 'di thams cad snang ba rgya chen pos gsal bar
16b4(mdo sde): gyur cig/ 'jig rten na 'jig rten gyi bar gyi mun pa mun nag smag du gyur pa gang du nyi ma dang / zla ba 'di ltar rdzu 'phrul che ba 'di ltar mthu che ba dag gis snang bar
16b5(mdo sde): mi nus pa de dag kyang de'i tshe snang ba chen pos gsal bar gyur to// der sems can gang dag skyes pa de dag rang gi lag pa brkyang pa yang mi mthong ba las// de
16b6(mdo sde): rnams snang ba des sems can gcig gis gcig mthong na/ shes ldan dag sems can gzhan yang 'dir skyes so zhes bya bar shes so// gang tshe rnam 'dran bltam/
16b7(mdo sde): par gyur pa na/ de tshe sa ni ring bcas shin du g.yo// gang gis 'jig rten par yang skad cig gis/ snang byed 'od ldan gsal de yang 'byung bar 'gyur/
16b8(mdo sde): de nas rgyal po zas gtsang mas sa g.yos pa chen po dang // stong ba chen po mthong ba dang byang chub sems dpa' la bskor ba byas te/ zhabs gnyis la phyag byas
17a1(mdo sde): nas 'di skad ces smras so// 'di lta bu'i rdzu 'phrul che ba dang / mthu che ba'i bu skyes pa ni bdag gis rnyed pa legs par rnyedo//
17a2(mdo sde): chos nyid kyi gang gi tshe byang chub sems dpa' shAkya thub pa yum gyi lhums nas bltam pa dang / ral gri shubs nas phyung ba bzhin du mngal gyi dri ma dang / sha ma'i dri ma
17a3(mdo sde): dang / khrag gi dri ma dang / mi gtsang ba gzhan dang gzhan sna tshogs kyis ma gos so// ji ltar 'od gsal tshon shel bzang po dang / ka shi ras gtsang phan tshun gos mi
17a4(mdo sde): 'gyur// de bzhin thub de lhums nas byung ba na/ gser spungs me chen nang nas bton pa 'dra/ chos nyid kyis byang chub sems dpa' shAkya thub pa yum gyi lhums nas
17a5(mdo sde): bltam pa de'i tshe/ de'i yum mi 'dug mi nyal te/ 'greng bzhin du rgyal rigs ma des rgyal rigs bsdam par byed do// de ni mi 'dug nyal ba'ang ma yin te/ yan
17a6(mdo sde): lag lnga ldan tshul khrims kyis brgyan pas/ de ni 'breng bzhin shin du dge ba yi/ gzhon nu de'i de brgya byin dag gi blangs/ chos nyid kyis gang gis tshe byang chub sems
17a7(mdo sde): dpa' shAkya thub pa yum gyi lhums nas bltam pa de'i tshe/ de'i dbu'i steng nas lham gdugs dkar po dang / nor bu'i yu ba can dag 'dzin to// dri med zla ba'i
17a8(mdo sde): dkyil 'khor 'od 'dra'i 'dugs/ lha'i rtse'i dbu'i steng nas 'dzin/ gdub 'khrol 'od zer gyis 'bar lag pa dang / rnga yab bzang gis 'di la g.yod
17b1(mdo sde): par byed/ chos nyid kyis gang gis tshe byang chub sems dpa' shAkya thub pa bltam pa'i mngol bar snang las chu gsil ba cig dang / chu dran mo cig ste/ chu gnyis
17b2(mdo sde): kyi rgyun smri gtsug gi steng du 'bab pa des byang chub sems dpa' khrus mdzad do// dri med rab dag bsil dang de bzhin rdo'i/ chu yis rkang gnyis gtso bo khrus mdzang
17b3(mdo sde): de// rigs rgyud gang du byang chub sems dpa' 'khrungs/ klu rnams de la mchod pa byed par gyur/ chos nyid kyis byang chub sems dpa' bltam pa'i mad
17b4(mdo sde): la skrun pa'i yum gyi mdun du chu mig chen po byung nas 'bab par gyur te/ de la de'i yum chus bya ba byed do// rkang gnyis gtso bo gzhon nu bltam pa na/
17b5(mdo sde): lha de rnams ni shin du yid dga' bas/ de rI chu bzang byung bar gyur pa la/ de yum der ni chus bya ba byed/ lha'i rol mo shin du sgra snyan rnams/ shin du
17b6(mdo sde): dga' ba mchog tu gdung bar byed/ de rnams gos dang phreng ba mthor byed cing / gzhan dag rab tu btud cing de bzhin bstod/ chos nyid kyis byang chub
17b7(mdo sde): sems dpa' bltam pa'i mad la/ sbas par snang las lha'i ud pa la dang / pad ma dang / ku mu ta dang / pad ma dkar po dang / a ka ru'i phye ma dang /
17b8(mdo sde): brgya spos kyi phye ma dang / tsan dan gyi phye ma dang / ta ma la'i 'dab mas 'thor ro// lha'i me tog man da rabs kyang mthor ro// lha'i sil snyan rnams kyang sna
18a1(mdo sde): 'byin to// gos rab dag kyang mthong bar byed/ mkhas pas btung ba'i sangs rgyas bltam pa na/ dri zhim dri mchog char ni phab ba dag
18a2(mdo sde): de dang des ni rab spobs chu la mthun pa'i/ rab dga'i sems kyis stod pa brjod par byed/ 'di ni byang chub mchog dag thob 'gyur zhing / sdug bsngal zad pa'i 'gro
18a3(mdo sde): phan mdzad 'gyur la/ 'gro ba mi shes rab rib mi mdongs la/ sman mchog 'di yis mig ni rab rtsol 'gyur/ 'di ni rmongs pas mig khyebs long ba'i/ 'gro
18a4(mdo sde): ba'i sgron ma chen po nyid du 'gyur/ lta ngan gyis brlag log pa'i lam zhugs la/ ma mdzol drang po'i lam ni ston par 'gyur/ ngan 'gro'i lam ni ma lus
18a5(mdo sde): 'gog 'gyur zhing / lha'i gnas kyis ni 'byed 'gyur zhes/ 'og man bar snang gnas pa'i lha rnams ni/ lha'i gnas su yang yang ba sgrogs par byed//
18a6(mdo sde): gang gi tshe byang chub sems dpa' shAkya thub pa bstam pa de nyid kyi tshe/ mnyan yod du rtsibs kyis 'phur/ tshangs byin bu bcas pa na tshangs byin 'di snyams du sems
18a7(mdo sde): te// bdag gi bu btsas pa na yul gsasmra ba bzhin du snang bas de bas na 'di'i ming gsal rgyal zhes bya ba btags so// rgyal po'i khab kyi grong khyer na
18a8(mdo sde): rgyal po pad ma chen po bu btsas pa na pad ma chen po 'di snyam du sems te/ bdag gi bu bcas pa na/ 'jig rten nyi ma'i gzugs shar ba ltar snang zhing
18b1(mdo sde): gzugs can ma'i bu yin pas 'di'i ming gzugs can snying po zhes bya bar gdags so// zhes btags so// ko'u sha ma bi na rgyal po dmag brgya bI bu bcas pa
18b2(mdo sde): na dmag brgya pa 'di snyams du sems te/ bdag gi bu btsas pa na 'jig rten nyi ma shar ba ltar snang bar gyur pas 'di'i ming shar ba zhes bya bar gdags so//
18b3(mdo sde): grong khyer 'phags rgyal du po mu khyud mtha' yas bu btsas pa na de 'di snyam du sems te/ bdag gi bu btsas pa na 'jig rten sgron mas snang ba lta bur gyur pas 'di'i
18b4(mdo sde): ming rab snang zhes bya bar gdags so zhes btags so// de ni de lta ma yin no// 'on kyang de thams cad byang chub sems dpa'i mthu yin no// gang gi tshe byang chub
18b5(mdo sde): sems dpa' shAkya thub pa bltam pa de nyid kyi dga'o las stsogs pa shAkya gzhon nu lnga brgya bcas pa dang / grags 'dzin ma las stsogs pa shAkya gzhon nu lnga brgya
18b6(mdo sde): brtsas pa dang / 'dun pa las sogs pa rim 'gro ba lnga brgya btsas pa dang / sngags ldan las stsogs pa rta lnga brgya 'brengaso// lha rnams kyis gter lnga'i kha yang
18b7(mdo sde): nye bar stan to// khams kyi rgyal phran rnams dang / mkhar gyi rgyal po rnams kyi rab tu btud cing thams cad kyis kyang dpya phul lo// de nas rgyal po zas gtsang ma 'di
18b8(mdo sde): snyam du sems te/ bdag gi bu btsas pa na 'dod pa thams cad grub pas na/ gzhon nu 'di'i ming don thams cad grub pa zhes bya'o// zhe byang chub sems dpa' la thog mar ma/
19a1(mdo sde): mngon#btags so// chos nyid kyi byang chub sems dpa' shAkya thub pa bltam pa'i modo la yab yum gyis mtshan mkhan dang ltas mkhan gyi bram
19a2(mdo sde): ze rnams la nye bar ston pa yin pas shes ldan dag cig gzhon nu gang dag dang ldan na/ 'gro ba gnyis su 'gyur gyi gzhan du ni ma yin te/ gal te khyim pa khyim pa na gnas par
19a3(mdo sde): 'gyur na/ 'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal po mtha' bzhir rnam rgyal ba chos kyi rgyal po chos dang ldan pa/ rin po che sna bdun dang ldan par 'gyur te/ de'i rin po che sna bdun ni 'di lta bu
19a4(mdo sde): dag 'byung ste/ 'di lta ste 'khor lo rin po che dang / glang po rin po che dang / rta rin po che dang / nor bu rin po che dang / bud med rin po che dang / khyim bdag rin po che dang / bdun po
19a5(mdo sde): ni blon po rin po che'o// bu dpa' ba rtul phod pa/ yan lag mchog gi gzugs dang ldan pa// pha rol gyi sde rab tu 'joms pa de rgya mtsho la thub pa'i sa blo ma lus par
19a6(mdo sde): gnod par sngo ba med cing mche ba med pa 'di nyid ched pa med cing mtshon gyis 'da' ba med la/ chos dang mthun pas legs par phab ste gnas par gyur to// gal te sgra
19a7(mdo sde): dang kha spu dregs nas gos ngur smrig dgos te/ dad pa yang dag pa kho nas khyim nas khyim med par rab tu byung na/ de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang blar rdzogs pa'i
19a8(mdo sde): sangs rgyas zhes bya bar 'jig rten du sgra rnam par grags par 'gyur ba skyes bu chen po'i mtshan sum bcu rtsa gnyis dang ldan nas/ lha mod lags te gzhon nu skyes bu chen po'i mtsha
19b1(mdo sde): sum bcu rtsa gnyis dang ldan pa ni/ 'gro ba gnyis su 'gyur gyi gzhan du ma yin te zhes bya ba nas/ yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas zhes bya bar 'jig rten du grags par
19b2(mdo sde): 'gyur zhes bya ba'i bar du ste snga ma bzhin du 'di ni 'dir chos nyid yin no// de la 'di skad ces bya ste/ rgyal pos gzhon nu ltam nas skyes bu'i mtshan shes bram ze la dris
19b3(mdo sde): te smras/ rgyal bu gal te khyim na gnas gyur na/ nges par 'di ni mi dbang dag tu 'gyur/ brtul bar ldan zhing rgyal po gzhan rnams kyi/ spyi la dbang ba'i 'khor/
19b4(mdo sde): los sgyur bar 'gyur/ 'di ni gling rnams kun du mngon rgyal ba'i/ chos kyi rgyal srid dag ni byed par 'gyur/ rin chen gyur pa 'di ni rin chen bdun/ mi mchog
19b5(mdo sde): bsod nams las kyis thob par 'gyur/ gang gis mthu yis sa ni ma lus pa/ 'di ni lus mi gcig pa spyod par 'gyur// gser las legs byas lte/
19b6(mdo sde): ba shin du zlum/ brtsibs stong ldan zhing mu khyud ma nyams bzang / dang por sa la rnam par rgyal 'gyur gang / 'khor lo de 'di dang por thob par 'gyur/ yan lag
19b7(mdo sde): thams cad legs skyes sa la ni/ rab gnas gangs can rtse 'dra'i glang po mchog/ rgyal po zla 'os mkha' la 'gro ba'i/ rin chen mchog ni gnyis pa 'dis thob
19b8(mdo sde): 'gyur/ tho rang dus su phyogs kun ma lus pa'i/ sa rnams bskor nas slar ni ldog gyur gang / rma bya'i mgrin 'dra spu ni yid 'ong ba'i/ rin chen rta ni 'di yis thob
20a1(mdo sde): mngan/ #par 'gyur/ rin chen dri med bai DUr rang bzhin/ kun du dpag tshad tsam du snang byed pa/ dri med mtshan mo ci 'dra nyid de bzhin/ rin chen mchog ni
20a2(mdo sde): bzhi pa 'thob par 'gyur/ gang zhig dri gzugs dang mdangs ldan pa'i/ bud med dam pa rigs ldan rnams kyi mchog/ lha mo bzhin du yon tan kun ldan pa/ bud med
20a3(mdo sde): rin chen deng 'dir 'thob par 'gyur/ gang yang 'di na rgyal la mu tig dang / gser stsogs shin du mang po 'bul ba'i/ nor ldan mtshungs par nor mang khyim bdag
20a4(mdo sde): ni/ rin chen thob nas rnam par spyod par 'gyur/ 'gro dang kun du gnas dang rnam ldog par/ ma lus dpung la mkhas par byed pa yi/ dpal ldan bdun po 'byung
20a5(mdo sde): bar 'gyur ba ni/ ma'i rin chen blon po zhes bya ba yin/ dpa' zhing rtul phod yan lag mchog gzugs ldan/ bu stong dag ni 'di la 'byung 'gyur zhing / gang gi
20a6(mdo sde): gzi brjid shin du stobs che zhing / sa bdag gzhan dag 'dud par byed par 'byung / gal te khyim ni nyes mang gis bkrugs pa/ rab 'bar shing ni bya yis spong
20a7(mdo sde): bltar/ nye bar zhi phyir nags su des song na/ deng 'dir ring por mi thogs sangs rgyas 'gyur/ khyed kyi sras 'di deng ni 'di 'dra ba/ gzhon nu 'gro ba'i rin chen
20a8(mdo sde): gcig lham pa/ 'gro ba gnyis las gzhan du mi 'gro bar/ de ltar sngags kyi tshig las mthong ba lags/ shes ldan dag gang dag dang ldan pa'i skyes bu
20b1(mdo sde): chen po'i 'gro ba gnyis su 'gyur gyi gzhan du ma yin zhes bya ba nas snga ma bzhin du 'jig rten gyi sgra rnam par grags par 'gyur/ zhes bya ba'i bar gyi skyes bu chen po'i mtshan
20b2(mdo sde): sum bcu rtsa gnyis po ni gang dag yin/ lha gzhon nu'i zhabs shin du gnas pa lags so// zhabs gnyis shin du gnas pa nyid kyis sa la mnyam par 'bab ste/
20b3(mdo sde): lha 'di ni gzhon nu'i skye bu chen po'i mtshan lags so// de'i zhabs kyi mthil gyi ngos gnyis la 'khor lo rtsibs stong pa lta ba dang / mu khyud du bcas pa rnam pa tham
20b4(mdo sde): cad yongs su rdzogs par mchis te/ lha 'di ni gzhon nu'i skyes bu chen po'i skyes bu'i mtshan lags so// lha gzhon nu'i sor mo ring ba dang / zhabs kyi ting pa
20b5(mdo sde): yangs dang / de'i phyag dang zhabs 'jams zhing gzhon sha chags pa lags te/ phyag dang zhabs 'jams zhing gzhon sha chags pa ni dper na shing bal gyi 'dab
20b6(mdo sde): ma 'am/ ras bal gyi 'dab ma bzhin no// lha 'di ni gzhon nu'i skye bu chen po'i skyes bu'i mtshan lags so// lha gzhon nu'i phyag dang zhabs/ dra bar 'brel
20b7(mdo sde): pa lags te/ de'i phyag dang zhabs dra bar 'brel ba ni dper na ngang po'i rgyal po gzhon nu bzhin no// lha 'di ni gzhon nu'i skyes bu chen po'i skye bu'i mtshan lags so//
20b8(mdo sde): lha gzhon nu'i zhabs long bu'i tshig mi mngon pa dang / byin pa ri dgas en ya lta bu dang / sku ma dub pa dang / sku bzhengs bzhin du ma btud par phyag pus ma'i
21a1(mdo sde): lhang gnyis brebs shing reg ste/ lha 'di ni gzhon nu'i skyes bu chen po'i mtshan lags so// lha gzhon nu ni 'doms kyi sba ba sbubs
21a2(mdo sde): su nub pa lags te/ de'i 'doms kyi sba ba sbubs su nub pa ni/ dper na glang po che cang shes kyi 'am/ rta cang shes byung ma thag gi bzhin no// lha 'di ni gzhon nu'i
21a3(mdo sde): skyes bu chen po'i mtshan lags so// lha gzhon nu'i sku ji srid par 'dom yang de srid la 'dom ci srid par sku yang de srid pas/ shing nu dro da ltar chu zheng gab pa lags
21a4(mdo sde): tau/ lha 'di ni gzhon nu'i skyes bu'i chen po'i mtshan lags so// lha gzhon nu'i ro stod kyi spu re re nas skye ba yang mthing ga la g.yas phyogs su 'khyil bar skye lags
21a5(mdo sde): te/ lha 'di ni gzhon nu'i skyes bu chen po'i mtshan lags so// lha gzhon nu ni mdog gser 'dra ba dang / 'od 'dom gang pa dang / lpags pa srab cing mdog
21a6(mdo sde): gser gyi dra ba lags te/ lpags pa srab pa nyid kyis rdul dang dri mas sku la mi gos pa ste/ lha 'di ni gzhon nu'i skyes bu chen po'i skyes bu chen po'i mtshan lags
21a7(mdo sde): so// lha gzhon nu'i sku ni bdun mtho ba ste/ sku bdun mtho bar 'khrungs pa ni phyag gnyis dang / zhabs gnyis dang / dpung mgo gnyis dang lhags pa lags
21a8(mdo sde): ke/ lha 'di ni gzhon nu'i skyes bu chen po'i mtshan lags so// su gzhon nu'i thal gong rgyas pa dang / skur stod seng ge'i 'dra ba dang / sru drang zhing khrom
21b1(mdo sde): che ba dang / dpung mgo shin du zlum pa dang / tshems bzhi bcu mnga' ba dang / tshems mnyam pa dang / tshems thags bzang ba dang / mche ba shin du dkar ba dang /
21b2(mdo sde): 'gram pa seng ge'i 'dra ba dang / ro bro ba'i mchog dang ldan pa lags te/ lha 'di ni gzhon nu'i skyes bu chen po'i skyes bu chen po'i mtshan lags so// lha gzhon nu ni
21b3(mdo sde): ljags shing du ring zhing srab pa lags te/ ljags shin du ring ba nyid dang / srab pa nyid kyi phyir/ ljags zhal nas phyung bas sgra mtshams nas bzung ste/
21b4(mdo sde): zhal gyi dkyil thams cad kyi ba du g.yog par mdzad pa ste/ lha 'di ni gzhon nu'i skyes bu chen po'i mtshan lags so// lha gzhon nu ni tshangs pa'i dbyangs dang /
21b5(mdo sde): ka la ping ka'i skad ltar yid du 'ong ba dang / nga'i dbyangs can rga lags te/ lha 'di ni gzhon nu'i skyes bu chen po'i mtshan lags so// lha gzhon nu ni spyan mthon ting
21b6(mdo sde): la ba'i rdzi ma lta bu dang / gtsug tor dang ldan pa dang / smin mtshams kyi mdzod spu dung ltar dkar zhing g.yas su 'khyil ba lags te/ lha 'di ni gzhon nu'i skyes
21b7(mdo sde): bu chen po'i skyes bu chen po'i mtshan lags so// lha 'di dag ni gang dag dang ldan pa'i 'gro ba gnyis su 'gyur gyi gzhan du ni ma lags pa zhes bya ba nas snga ma bzhin
21b8(mdo sde): du 'jig rten du sgra rnam par grags par 'gyur ro// zhes bya ba'i bar gyi skyes bu chen po'i mtshan sum bcu rtsa gnyis lags so// bdag nyid legs bsgom
22a1(mdo sde): mnganasku la ni/ sku'i tha ma 'dzin mdzad pa'i/ thub pa chen po'i mtshan rnams ni/ de ni bdag gis brjod par bgyi/ 'di zhabs shin
22a2(mdo sde): du gnas pa ste/ sa la mnyam par 'bab pa yin/ 'di zhabs phyags gi mthil la ni/ 'khor lo shin du dbyibs legs skyes// 'di zhabs gting ba yangs pa
22a3(mdo sde): dang / de ni sor mo ring zhing mdzes/ phyag zhabs dra bas 'brel ba dang / shing bal lta bur 'jam pa dang / 'di zhabs long bu'i tshigs mi mngon/ byin pa e na ya
22a4(mdo sde): dang / mtshungs/ mi mchog sku yang ma btud par/ phyag gis pus mo'i lha nga sleb/ 'doms kyi sba ba sbubs su nub/ nu dro da ltar chu zheng gab/ ro stod spu ni re re nas/
22a5(mdo sde): skye zhing de spu g.yas su 'khyil/ mdog ni gser sbyangs 'dra ba dang / kun nas 'dom gang 'od dang ldan/ bcom ldan de'i lpags srab cing / 'di sku bdun ni mtho
22a6(mdo sde): ba ste/ bcom ldan thal gong rgyas pa dang / sku stod seng ge 'dra ba dang / sku drang kho lag che ba dang / dbu mgo shin du zlum pa dang / bcu phrag bzhi'i tshems
22a7(mdo sde): rnams ni/ yongs su rdzogs shing ma tshang med/ mnyam dang thags bzang nyid du ni/ de yi tshems ni legs par gnas/ rab dkar 'gram pa seng ge 'dra//
22a8(mdo sde): ro bro mchog dang ldan pa dang / ljags ni shin du srab pa dang / bcom ldan tshangs pa'i dbyangs dang ldan/ rdzi ma pa spyan mthon thing dang / smin ma'i mtshams kyi mdzod/
22b1(mdo sde): sku ni/ dung ltar dkar zhing g.yas su 'khyil/ mtshan bzangs sum bcu rtsa gnyis 'di/ gang zhig la ni 'byung 'gyur ba/ de ni 'gro ba gnyis 'gyur gyi/ gsum
22b2(mdo sde): par 'gyur ba ma lags so// 'di ni gal te khyim gnas na/ 'khor los sgyur rgyal nyid 'gyur te/ dran ldan bu ni mang ba dang / gnod pa chung zhing mkhas par
22b3(mdo sde): 'gyur/ gal te rab byung rdzogs sangs rgyas/ gang zag mnyam pa med par 'gyur/ bshos dang btung dang na bza' dang / gzims cha rnams kyang rnyed 'gyur
22b4(mdo sde): la/ 'di yi 'khor ni mi byed cing / lus can kun gyi yid du 'od/ lha rnams rjes su 'brang ba dang / mi rnams kyang ni de bzhin te/ chos kyi bdag po mchog gyur zhing /
22b5(mdo sde): mi yul dag tu yang de bzhin 'gyur/ mnyam pa med cing 'dra ba med/ rnams 'dren mtshungs pa med par 'gyur/ lha 'di ni gzhon nu'i skyes bu chen po'i mtshan lags
22b6(mdo sde): te/ gang dang ldan na 'gro ba gnyis su 'gyur gyi gzhan du ni ma lags zhes bya ba ni snga ma bzhin no// chos nyid kyi byang chub sems dpal shAkya thub pa ltam nas//
22b7(mdo sde): zhag bdun lon pa dang / de skrun pa'i yum nongs par 'gyur te/ nong ma thag tu sum bcu rtsa gsum gyi lha'i ris gya nom par skyes so// de nas rgyal po zas gtsang
22b8(mdo sde): mas byang chub sems dpa' ma ma rnams la gtad nas/ ma ma khyod kyis gzhon nu 'di dus dus su sku mnye gyi shig dus dus su khrus byos shig/ dus dus su zas byin cig/
23a1(mdo sde): / dus dus su yang dag pa'i bde bas bsnyen bskur byos shig ma ma dga' ba'i lag pa gnyis kyi de blangs nas/ dus dus su skum nye byang / dus dus
23a2(mdo sde): su yang dag pa'i bde bas bsnyen bskur byed do// yang de'i tshe dri shin du yid du 'ong ba'i ngo bo gang yin pa de rnams kyis byugs shing rgyan thams cad kyis brgyan nas yab zas
23a3(mdo sde): gtsang gis de blangs te/ dga' bas phang du bzhag nas yang du rtog cing dga' ba skyed do// chos nyid kyis byang chub sems dpa' shAkya thub pa ni gzugs bzang ba/ mdzes
23a4(mdo sde): pa lta na sdug pa/ mi yi khog las yang dag par 'das la/ lha'i kha dog ma thob pa skyes pa dang bud med rnams kyis ltas pa na/ ngoms mi shes shing dga' ba thob te/
23a5(mdo sde): dper na 'dzam bu'i chu bo'i gser las mgar ba mkhas brgyan rdungs pa/ la ba dkar sar ba'i steng du bzhag na shin du gsal zhing 'bar la rnam par mtsher ba de bzhin du
23a6(mdo sde): byang chub sems dpa' shAkya thub pa gzugs bzang ba/ mdzes pa lta na sdug pa/ mi'i kha dog las 'das shing / lha'i kho dog ni ma thob pa yin no// chos nyid kyis
23a7(mdo sde): byang chub sems dpa' shAkya thub pa skye bo tshogs chen po'i snying du sdug pa dang / yid du 'ong bar 'gyur te/ yang 'di skye bo'i tshogs chen pos de phrag pa nas phrag par
23a8(mdo sde): spong bar byed pa ni/ dper na ston ka'i pad ma skye bo'i tshogs chen po'i snying du sdug cing yid du 'ong bas skye bo'i chen po'i de lag pa nas lag par brgyud par byed pa
23b1(mdo sde): bzhin te/ snga ma bzhin no// chos nyid kyis byang chub sems dpa' ltam pa'i ma nas/ spyan mi 'dzums par gzugs rnams la lta ste/ de spyan mi 'dzums pa ni dper na/
23b2(mdo sde): sum bcu rtsa gsum gyi lha rnams bzhin no// chos nyid kyis byang chub sems dpa' ltam pa'i mad nas/ sngon gyi las kyi rnam par smin pa las skyes pa'i lha'i spyan dang / des
23b3(mdo sde): na de nyid dang mtshan du dpag tshad cig kho ra khor yug tu gzigs so// las bcas las byung dri med spun gyis ni/ gzugs chen po dang de bzhin phra rab rnams/ nyid dang
23b4(mdo sde): dang mtshan du khor yug dpag tshad cig/ mdun na gnas pa bzhin du'ang gzigs par gyur/ chos nyid kyi byang chub sems dpa' bltam pa'i mdo nas gsung snyan cing
23b5(mdo sde): 'jebs pa dang / gsung snyan pa dang / gsung yid du 'ong ba yin te/ dper na/ gang can gyi bya skad snyan cing 'jebs pa dang / skad snyan pa dang / yid du 'ong ba de
23b6(mdo sde): bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' bltam pa'i mod nas/ gsung snyan cing 'jebs pa dang / gsung yid du 'ong ba yin no// ri 'o kun 'dzin la drang srong nyon mongs med ces
23b7(mdo sde): bya ba mngon par shes pa lnga dang ldan pa byams pa'i bdag nyid can snying rje dang ldan pa/ skye dgul mnyes shin pa zhig gnas te/ de la tshe'o mi sbyin zhes bya ba yod pa
23b8(mdo sde): dang / de de'i tshe phug tu zhugs te bsams gtan byed pa na byang chub sems dpa' bltam ste/ 'jig rten thams cad snang ba rgya chen pos gsal bar gyur pa'i
24a1(mdo sde): snang ba de mthong ba dang / nyon mongs med la smras pa/ mkhan po 'dir ni nyi ma thams cad dag/ cig car byung bar 'gyur ram ci/ 'di ska
24a2(mdo sde): ri ni phug bcas pa/ 'di ni 'od gyis gsal bar gyur/ nyon mongs med de smras pa/ nyi ma'i 'od ni rgyun du no// bu cig snang ba 'di dag ni/ yan lag reg na 'od
24a3(mdo sde): gsal bas/ nges par thub pa de'i 'od/ byang chub sems dpa' 'od chen ni/ nges par lhums nas ltam gyur la/ lham nas sems dpa' chen po de'i/ 'od gzer gse
24a4(mdo sde): dang 'dra ba ni/ dri ma med pa 'di dag gis/ 'jig rten gsum ni snang byas yin/ mes sbyin gyis smras pa mkhan po bzhud/ ci re zhig 'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal por
24a5(mdo sde): 'gyur ram/ 'on te bla na med pa'i ye shes rtogs par 'gyur ba rang nyid lta bar mdzod cig/ drang srong nyon mongs med kyis smras pa/ da lta ni rgyal po zas gtsang ma'i khyim
24a6(mdo sde): nyi 'od kyi rgyal po dang / mkhar gyi rgyal po dang / tshong pa dang tshong dpon dang / ded dpon rnams dang / bram ze dang / khyim bdag brgya stong dpag tu med pas
24a7(mdo sde): kun du khyab nas/ 'dug gis gang gis che de dben par gyur pa de'i tshe rgyal po zas gtsang ma'i gan du 'gro bar bya'o// de nas rgyal po zas gtsang ma 'di snyam du skye ma'o
24a8(mdo sde): drang srong nyon mongs med rkang gis ser skye'i gzhir 'ongs na ci ma rung snyam du sems so// de nas drang srong nyon mongs med steng gi nam mkha' la mngon par 'phags
24b1(mdo sde): nas rgyal po zas gtsang ma'i pho brang sgor phyin pa dang / ji tsam na sgo srungs kyis rgyal po zas gtsang ma la lha dgyes pa bskyed du gsol/ drang srong nyon mongs/
24b2(mdo sde): med 'dir mchis so zhes rig par byas pa dang / rgyal po bzas gtsang mas thos te/ dga' ba dang / mgu ba dang / rab tu dga' ba dang / mchog tu rangs
24b3(mdo sde): pas byung nas mchog tu gus pas mchog de skad ces smras so// drang srong chen po legs par 'ongs so// dgos pa ci zhig la 'ongs/ nyon mongs med kyis smras
24b4(mdo sde): pa/ rgyal po chen po bdag ni 'dir/ khyed sras lta ba'i phyir mchis te/ 'jig rten gtso bo rnams 'dren pa/ thub pa de ni mthong bar 'tshal/ rgyal pos smras
24b5(mdo sde): pa/ gal te de lta na ni gzhon nu ga nyid log gis/ sad kyi bar du re shig sdod cig/ nyon mongs med kyis smras pa/ rigs dang ldan pa'i lha rnams ni/ mtshan mo'i zhi
24b6(mdo sde): cha nyal ba ltar/ dgos pa don gnyer rnams kyi gnyid/ mig la yun rangs mi gnas so// de nas gzhon nu shAkya thub pa ma ma'i phang na 'dug pa drang srong nyon mongs
24b7(mdo sde): med la byin pa dang / drang srong nyo mos med kyis lag pa gnyis kyis blangs nas yud tsam rtag te smras pa/ lha gzhon nu 'di mtshan mkhan rnams kyis ji skad lung
24b8(mdo sde): stan/ rgyal po zas gtsang mas smras pa/ rin po che sna bdun dang ldan pa'i 'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal por 'gyur ro zhes zer ro// de nas drang srong nyon mongs
25a1(mdo sde): nomed kyis byang chub sems dpa' mthong nas tshigs su bcad de smras pa/ sa bdag rtogs pa po rnams blo 'khrul te/ rtsod pa'i dus na 'khor
25a2(mdo sde): lo la sgyur mi 'byung / bsod nams mchog gi chos kyi brjod 'di ni/ nyes las rnam par rgyal nas sangs rgyas 'gyur/ mtshan mi gsal dang ldan na mi dbang po/
25a3(mdo sde): gling bzhi rnams kyi bdag po dbang phyug 'gyur/ thub dbang mtshan ni shin du gsal bas na/ mi mchog sangs rgyas chos kyi 'khor lo sgyur/ de nas drang srong nyon mongs
25a4(mdo sde): med kyis bdag nyid tshe'i mtha'i nges pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' mngon par byang chub pa rtag pa la zhugs pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' lo nyi shu rtsa dgu bzhes
25a5(mdo sde): nas khab nas byung nas/ lo drug tu dka' ba spyod par 'gyur te/ de nas bdud rtsi rtogs par 'gyur ba mthong ngo // bdag ni bar skabs der mchi ba'i dus byed
25a6(mdo sde): par mthong nas/ de mig mchi mas gang te 'dug pa rgyal po zas gtsang gis mthong nas/ sngags nas tshigs su bcad de smras pa/ skyes pa bud med rnams kyis
25a7(mdo sde): mthong ba na/ ngoms pa mi 'gyur dga' ba 'thob 'gyur ba/ lus bzang dge byed de ni 'dir mthong nas/ drang srong chen po ci'i slad du bzhin 'gyur/ ga las bdag gi
25a8(mdo sde): gzhon nu 'jigs pa 'am/ tshe zad 'gyur ba nye bar mi gnas dang / de ni myur du legs par bdag la spros/ khyod kyis mchi mas bdag ni dngang bar 'gyur/
25b1(mdo sde): drang srong nyon mongs med kyis tshigs su bcad de smras pa// gal te 'di'i stengadu na mkha' las// rdo rje ser drag 'phangs par ba' gyur kyang // thub pa chen po'i sku
25b2(mdo sde): la ba spu ni// nyag ma cig kyang g.yos par mi nus so// me chen rlung gi shugs kyis bdas pa dang // mtshon cha rnon po shin du mi zad dang // drag po'i dug dang sbrul
25b3(mdo sde): gyi dug rnon yang // gzhon nu la ba ba skad cig 'jig mi 'gyur// thugs rje nyid las gnas gyur gang lags pa// 'jigs pas nyen pa rnams la mi 'jigs stsa//
25b4(mdo sde): de ni 'jigs pa kun gyi 'jigs 'joms na// mi dbang 'di la 'jig pa ga la 'byung // 'jig rten na ni bdag nyid che rnams kyi/ gtsor gyur bdag nyid chen po gang
25b5(mdo sde): zhig la// tshangs bcas lha yang rtag tu srung byed pa// mi dbang 'di la 'jigs pa ga la 'byung // mi dbang bdag ni rgud pa mthong nas ni// gang phyir zhi ba mi thob bdag
25b6(mdo sde): tu med// chos kyi mchog mdzod 'dri phrad nas ni// don ma thob par bdag ni mchi bar 'gyur// gang dag smra ba dam pa mtshungs med pa// 'di'i chos thos 'gyur zhing
25b7(mdo sde): thob nas kyang // rab tu zhi ba'i pha rol 'gro de dag/ skyid cing bsod nams ldan la rims nad bral// de nas drang srong nyon mongs med byang chub sems dpa' reg/
25b8(mdo sde): pa'i mthus de'i rdzu 'phrul nyams so// nyams pa dang nyon mongs med kyis smras pa// rkang pa kho na nas grong khyer nas phyir 'byung bar bya'o// de nas rgyal
26a1(mdo sde): mngon/ zas gtsang mas thos nas/ grong khyer thams cad kyi rdo ba dang / gseg ma dang / gyo mo rnams bsal nas spos dang phye mas
26a2(mdo sde): khyab par byed du bcug go// de nas drang srong nyon mongs med 'byor pa chen pos grong khyer nas byung ste rim gyis ri'o kun 'dzin du phyin pa dang / mi sbyin la smras pa// ngas
26a3(mdo sde): gzhon nu mthong ste/ bla na med pa'i yes shes rtogs par 'gyur na/ ngas ni de sleb par mi 'gyur te/ nga ni bar skabs su dus byed par 'gyur gyis/ khyod ni de'i
26a4(mdo sde): thad du rab tu byung la/ nga rgyal dang dregs pa nyes par bcom par 'gyur ba dang / tshangs par spyod pa la spyad par byas te/ rigs kyis dregs par mi bya/ rus kyis
26a5(mdo sde): dregs par mi bya/ rigs rgyud kyis dregs par mi bya ste/ khyod kyis kyang yun ring po mi thogs par bdud rtsi 'thob par 'gyur gyis zhes smras nas/ yang tshigs
26a6(mdo sde): su bcad de smras pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa tshol 'dod na/ shar phyogs su ni khyod 'dug na/ rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas drags ldan pa/ rnyed par dka' ba mthong bar
26a7(mdo sde): 'gyur/ de nas dus gzhan zhig nas/ rgyal po zas gtsang mas gzhon nu ma ma'i pha ngan 'dug pa la yang dang yang du lta zhing nga'i bu ce 'dra ba de lta bu ni sa'i steng na su la
26a8(mdo sde): yang med do// snyam du sems shing shin du dga' bar gyur to// de nas byang chub sems dpa' 'khrungs nas ring po ma lon par ma ma'i pang du bzhugs nas gser
26b1(mdo sde): gyi gnong par 'bras dang sha bsregs pa'i chan gsol ba na/ de ma mas bkab kyang ma thub par mang por gsol nas 'phrog par brtsams pa dang / 'phrog
26b2(mdo sde): ma nus nas des rgyal po zas gtsang la sbran pa dang / rgyal po btsun mo dang lhan cig gis 'phrog par brtsams pa dang des kyang ma nus so// de nas rgyal po blon
26b3(mdo sde): po rnams ser spyan gnas pa'i skye bo'i tshogs rnams la bsgo na de rnams kyis kyang 'phrog par ma nus so// de nas glang po che lnga brgya la btags pa dang / byang chub
26b4(mdo sde): sems dpas 'di rnams kyis bdag gi stobs nyams na mi rung gis/ ma la bdag gis 'dzub mo bkug nas gser gyi gzhod pa nas bzung ngo snyam nas des
26b5(mdo sde): 'dzub mo bkug pas gser gyi gnod pa gzung nas drangs pa dang / glang po che lnga brgya po de dag kha phyir sgyur te drangs nas de dag gis kyang gser gyi gzhong
26b6(mdo sde): pa 'phrog par ma nus so// rgyal po zas gtsang gis bsams pa ji ltar byang chub sems dpa'i lag pa g.yon pas glang po che lnga brgya drangs pa dang sbyar na/
26b7(mdo sde): gdon mi za bar lag pa gnyis kyis ni glang po che stong thub kyis de bas na gzhon nu'i ming glang po che stong gi stobs can zhes bdags so// grong khyer sor skya'i
26b8(mdo sde): gzhi na gnod sbyin ni shAkya 'phel zhes bya ba zhig smug mar gnas so// shAkya rnams kyis kun du spyod pa ni/ shAkya su yang rung ba la khye'u 'am/ bum
27a1(mdo sde): btsas pa gang yin pa de gnod sbyin shAkya 'phel gyi rkang pa la phyag 'tshal du bzhugs pa'i phyir khrid pa yin pas/ rgyal pos
27a2(mdo sde): blon po rnams la bsgo ba/ shes ldan dag deng la gzhon nu gnod sprin shAkya 'phel gyi rkang pa la phyag 'tshal du chug shig/ de nas byang chub sems dpa' glang po che la skyon
27a3(mdo sde): te// dpung gi tshogs dpag tu med pas yongs su bskor te// grong khyer ser skya'i gzhir 'jug par brtsams pa dang // grong khyer ser skya'i bzhi sgra bcu gnyis dang bral
27a4(mdo sde): bar gyur cig byang chub sems dpa' de nang du zhugs pa na thub pa bzhin du gnas par gyur to// de nas rgyal po zas gtsang mas bsams pa/ grong khyer 'di lta ste
27a5(mdo sde): glang po che'i sgra dang / rta'i sgra dang / shing rta'i sgra dang / dpung bu chung gi sgra dang / dung gi sgra dang / rnga bo che'i sgra dang / pe ta'i sgra dang / ra dung gi sgra dang /
27a6(mdo sde): grar gi sgra dang / glu'i sgra dang / rol mo'i sgra dang / sbyin pa ni byin/ bsod nams ni gyis/ bsnyen gnas la ni nye bar gnas/ tshul khrims yang dag
27a7(mdo sde): par blabs te gnas shing ces bya ba'i sgra ste/ bcu gnyis dang bral zhing gzhon nu de nang du zhugs pa na thub pa bzhin du zhi bar gnas pas/ gzhon nu'i ming ni shAkya
27a8(mdo sde): thub pa zhes btags so// zhes byang chub sems dpa'i ming shAkya thub pa zhes bya bar btags so// / de nas byang chub sems dpa' gnod sbyin shAkya 'phel gyi
27b1(mdo sde): gan du khyer ba dang / gnod sbyin shAkya 'phel gyis byang chub sems dpa' gnas dang nye bar phyin par mthong ngo // mthong nas kyang phyir byung nas/ lus thams/
27b2(mdo sde): kyis byang chub sems dpa'i rkang pa gnyis la gtugs te phyag byas so// de mthong ba dang rgyal po zas gtsang mas smras pa/ lhas kyang rkang pa gnyis la
27b3(mdo sde): gtugs pa 'di ni lha'i yang lha yin pas/ gzhon nu'i ming yang lha zhes bya'o// byang chub sems dpa'i ming lha'i yang lha zhes bya bar gtags so// de nas
27b4(mdo sde): de'i tshe rgyal po zas gtsang gis dgos pa'i ched la 'dug nas/ don zab mo tshigs dang yi ge dag shes rab kyis so sor 'byed par byed do// de nas byang chub
27b5(mdo sde): sems dpa' shAkya thub pa 'khor lnga brgya dang yi ge'i slob dpon srid bu go cha la yi ge slob par btang nas yi ge'i slob dpon rjon dpan srin bu go bcas byang chub sems
27b6(mdo sde): dpa' la yi ger bris nas phog pa dang / byang chub sems dpas smras pa/ 'di ni ngas shes so// de nas de yi ge gnyis dang gsum nas de
27b7(mdo sde): bzhin du lnga brgya'i bar bris nas phog pa dang / byang chub sems dpas smras pa// 'di dag thams cad kyang ngas shes kyis gzhan dag spros shig/ srin po bu
27b8(mdo sde): go cas smras pa/ 'jig rten ni yi ge 'di tsam spyod kyi/ gzhan ni bdag gis ma 'tshal to// de nas byang chub sems dpa' nyid kyis yi ge bris te/ srin bu go
28a1(mdo sde): do/ go cha la byin nas gsungs pa/ yi ge 'di'i ming ci yin smros shig/ de nas smras pa/ ma tshal to// byang chub sems dpas
28a2(mdo sde): gsungs pa/ 'jig rten du gnyis shig byung na mngon par 'gyur te/ byang chub sems dpa' 'khor los sgyur ba'o// na mkha'i ngos la gnas pa'i tshangs pas smras pa/
28a3(mdo sde): srin bu go ca byang chub sems dpa' ji skad gsungs pa de de bzhin te/ yi ge 'di ni 'jig rten du gnyis shig byung na mngon par 'gyur te/ byang chub sems dpa' 'am
28a4(mdo sde): 'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal po'o// byang chub sems dpas yi ge de tshangs pa'i dbyangs kyis dpags la na mkha'i ngos la gnas pa tshangs pas dbang byas pas
28a5(mdo sde): tshangs pa'i yi ge zhes bya ba gyur to// de nas byang chub sems dpa' yi ge'i mthar byin pa dang / 'khor lnga brgya dang bcas par bzang len dang lhar bcas zhes bya ba
28a6(mdo sde): 'phong gi slob dpon gyi gan du 'phong gi gnas su btud do// de nas byang chub sems dpa' gnas lnga po brgyad nas phog pa dang / sgra grag par phog pa dang / gan
28a7(mdo sde): du phog pa dang / mi mtsho bar phog pa dang / tsha bas tshe ba la byang bar gyur to// de nas bzang len dang lhar bcas 'di snyam du sems te/ byang chub sems dpa'
28a8(mdo sde): 'di ni snying rje can yin pas bslab par bya thams cad bslab kyi lha sbyin 'di ni bdug pa yin pas 'jig rten thams cad du gnod par 'gyur na mi rung gis 'di la gan du
28b1(mdo sde): du snun pa brlab par mi bya'o// de nas dus gzhan zhig na lha sprin gyis ngang pa lcags mangs bsnun pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' steng gi khang bzangs kyi gzhi
28b2(mdo sde): la bzhugs pa de'i phang par de lhung ngo // de nas byang chub sems dpas bzung nas mda' phyung ste sman gyis byug pas sos so// lhas byin gyis smras pa/ byang
28b3(mdo sde): chub sems dpa' dang pa 'di ni ngas yongs su bzung ba yin gyis bskur cig/ byang chub sems dpas smras pa/ ngas cher sngar yongs su bzung ste gang gi tshe bla
28b4(mdo sde): na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub du sems bskyed pa de kho na'i tshe yongs su bzung ngo // de byang chub sems dpa' la lha byin gnod sems dang / bzod
28b5(mdo sde): pa ma yin pa dang / phebs pa ma yin pa byung bar gyur te/ de nas lha byin la sogs shAkya'i gzhon nu lnga brgya byung ba dang / lha byin ras kyis bcings nas shAkya'i
28b6(mdo sde): gzhon nu lnga brgya skyel to// ci tsam na byang chub sems dpa' phyogs der bzhud pa dang / lha byin gyis smras pa/ byang chub sems dpa' ci la bstod/ byang chub
28b7(mdo sde): sems dpas kyang ras bcings te/ shAkya'i gzhon nu lnga brgya bsgyel to// de nas lha byin ras kyis bcings pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' bzung ste rkang pa gyen du
28b8(mdo sde): brtan nas gang rgyal du skyel ba dang // der yang byang chub sems dpa' la lha byin gnod sems dang / mi bzod pa dang / bag mi phebs pa'i sems gnyis pa bskyed par gyur to//
29a1(mdo sde): non/ bya/ de nas shakya gzhon nu lnga brgya mda' gzhu thogs te/ phyi rol du byung nas ta la la tshabs byed pa la zhugs pa dang / la las ni ta la cig/
29a2(mdo sde): phebs so// la las ni gnyis so// lha sprin gyis ni gsum mo// byang chub sems dpa' lcags mda' 'phangs pa dang / shing ta la bdun phigs pa las khyi srid
29a3(mdo sde): rlung gis skyod do// thams cad 'gyel ba'i bar du brgya cher sbyar ro// de nas gnas gtsang ma'i lha rnams 'bab chu ro ha ti ka'i 'gram na shing dge ba'i snying po zhes bya ba nyi
29a4(mdo sde): ma gcig cing khru rgyar skye ba/ mtshan mo ni sen mos kyang bcad du rung la/ nyin par ni mtshon gyis kyang gcad par mi nus pa zhig yod pa dang / gnas gtsang ma'i lha
29a5(mdo sde): rnams kyis gang gis shing dge ba'i snying po rtsa ba steng du gton nas/ ro ha ti'i nang na bcug pa de lta bu'i rlung dang char drug cig sprul to// de rgyal po zas gtsang ma dang
29a6(mdo sde): legs par rab sad kyis thos nas shing 'dis gong khyer brlab par ma gyur tam snyam nas srog chags brgya stong dpag tu med pa dang / shing dge ba'i snying po gang na ba der
29a7(mdo sde): song ste phyin pa dang / 'khor brgya stong dpag tu med pas drangs su zin kyang ci tsam na bskyod par yang ma nus so// 'char kas smras pa/ lha byang chub sems
29a8(mdo sde): dpa' sbron cig/ rgyal pos smras pa/ khu'o gzhon nu la bka' stsol bar mi nus so// 'char kas smras pa/ khyed rnams kyis ca tsa'i sgra gsang mthon po
29b1(mdo sde): sgrogs shing / ci nas kyang ngas byang chub sems dpa' gshegs par bya'o// de nas skye bo'i tshogs de rnams kyis sgra gsang mthon po dang / chen po'i ca co'i
29b2(mdo sde): sgra bsgrags so// 'char ka byang chub sems dpa'i thad du song ba dang / byang chub sems dpas smras pa/ 'char ka ca co'i sgra 'di ci zhig yin 'char kas
29b3(mdo sde): rnams pa de dag ba rgya cher gsol to// de nas byang chub sems dpas gsungs pa/ gal te lta na 'byin du 'deng / de nas 'char ka dang byang chub sems dpa' chas
29b4(mdo sde): pa dang / ci tsam na khung nas sbrul gdug pa zhig byung ngo // 'char kas byang chub sems dpa' zin par gyur du 'ong ngo zhes ral gri rnon pos rked pa gcad pa dang / sprul
29b5(mdo sde): gyis dug gi dbugs kyis char ka la phog ste/ de nas nag por gyur nas de'i ming yang 'char ka nag po zhes bya bar 'gyur ro// de nas byang chub sems dpa' shing dge
29b6(mdo sde): ba'i snying po gang na ba der bzhud de byon pa dang / lha byin la gsungs pa/ khyod kyi stobs ji tsam pa lta yis bskyod cig/ lha sprin gyi 'bad de cung zad cig bskal
29b7(mdo sde): lo// dga' bos ni cung zad drangs so// ji tsam na byang chub sems dpa' stobs kyi nyams sod par mdzad cing shing dge ba'i snying po phyag gis blangs te/ 'bab chu ro//
29b8(mdo sde): ha ha ka'i 'gram nas 'phangs te/ byang chub sems dpas gsungs pa shing ldan dge ba'i snying po 'di ni bsil ba'i rang bzhin yin pas 'khris pa'i nang dang shu ba dang / zam
30a1(mdo sde): mig byung ba la byug na zhi bar 'gyur gyis dum bur byos la khyer te rang rang gis khyim du zhog shig/ yangs pa can du glang po/
30a2(mdo sde): rin po che zhig skyes pa dang / de nas yangs pa can gyi li tsa byi rnams kyis glang po che mtshan dang ldan pa zhig rnyed nas/ de rnams kyi bsams pa rgyal po zas gtsang gi
30a3(mdo sde): sras mtshan mkhan rnams kyis 'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal por 'gyur ro// zhes lung snyan pa de'i mthus glang po rin po che 'di byung gis dong la de kho na la 'bul lo snyam
30a4(mdo sde): mo// de rnams kyis glang po che nga rgyan thams cad kyi brgyan nas khrid de dong ba las rim gyis ser skya'i bzhir phyin nas/ rgyal po'i pho brang gi sgor glang po che'i dam
30a5(mdo sde): pa gzhag nas sdong pa dang / ma stes te gdug pa'i las can lha sprin phyir byung ba des glang po che'i dam pa de de ltar rgyan gyis rgyan par mthob nas/ de des phrag
30a6(mdo sde): dog chen po skyes te/ de phrag dog dang mi bzod pa skyes pas dris pa/ glang po che'i dam pa 'di su'i yin/ de rnams kyis smras pa/ gzhon nu shAkya thub pa
30a7(mdo sde): mtshan mkhan rnams kyis 'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal por lung snyan pa de la yang yangs pa can gyis tshogs rnams kyis glang po rin po che 'di skyes su 'bul lo//
30a8(mdo sde): lhas sbyin lhag par mi bzod pa skyes nas smras pa/ res shig de 'khor los sgyur bar ma gyur pa/ je khyed cag glang por rini po che 'bul lam zhes smras nas/
30b1(mdo sde): thal lcag gis glang po che bsad do// ji tsam na phyogs der dga'o 'ongs pa de mthong nas dris pa/ shes ldan dag glang po che bzang po 'di sus bsad/ de rnams kyis
30b2(mdo sde): smras pa/ lha sbyin gyis so// nges bsam pa gdon mi za bar 'di la lhas sbyin gyis mthu sad kyis ma la bdag gis kyang 'di la mthu sad par bya'o// snyam nas
30b3(mdo sde): 'jug ma nas bzung gom pa bdun bor ro// ji tsam na byang chub sems dpa' shAkya thub pa phyir byung ba des de gzigs nas dris pa/ glang po che 'di gang nas zho
30b4(mdo sde): de rnams kyis ji ltar gyur pa smras so// sus bsad/ lha sbyin gyis so// 'gron rnams la 'gron gyi mchod pa bya ba yin na ma legs pa zhig byas so//
30b5(mdo sde): phyogs gang du bsad pha gir ro// 'dir sus drud/ dga' bos so// des dgongs pa 'dir gdon mi za bar de gnyis kyis 'di la mthu sad kyis ma la ngas kyang
30b6(mdo sde): 'di la mthu sad par bya'o// snyam du dgongs nas 'jug ma nas bzung ster ba'i khar 'phangs pa las ra ba'i rim pa bdun dang / 'o bas rim pa bdun las bzlas
30b7(mdo sde): ste bor ro// de lhung bas gshod btod pa glang po che'i gshong glang po che'i gshong zhes bya bar gyur to// 'dir smras pa/ lha sbyin gyis ni de na glang po che
30b8(mdo sde): bsad/ dga' bos de ni gom pa bdun du drung / byang chub sems dpas phyag gis bar snang la/ rdo ba bzhin du phyi rol rgyang ring 'phangs/ mtshan
31a1(mdo sde): mngonamakhan rnams kyis lung snyan pa/ gal te gzhon nu lo bcu gnyis kyi bar du rab tu ma byung na/ 'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal por/
31a2(mdo sde): 'gyur ro// de nas rgyal po zas gtsang ma 'di snyam du sems te/ ma la bdag gis 'di la 'dod pa'i yon tan lnga phal che byin na ni de rnams la dga' bas rab tu 'byung
31a3(mdo sde): bar mi 'gyur ro snyams nas/ rgyal po zas gtsang gis byang chub sems dpa'i mdun du gos dang rgyan gyi phung po gzhag nas smras pa/ deng khyed kyis shAkya'i bu mo rnams
31a4(mdo sde): la rgyan dang gos rnams byin cig/ de nas rgyal po zas gtsang gis ser skya'i grong khyer du deng gzhon nu gos dang rgyan rnams gnyen par 'gyur gyis shAkya'i bu mo thams cad
31a5(mdo sde): shog shig/ ces dril sgrog du bcug go// de nas shAkya gzhon nu ma lnga brgya 'ongs nas/ thams cad la byang chub sems dpas gos dang brgyan rnams byin no//
31a6(mdo sde): de nas shAkya dbyig pa can la grags 'dzin ma zhes bya ba'i bu mo yod pa dang des de la smras pa/ khyed la yang gzhon nu gos dang brgyan rnams ster bar 'gyur gyis so//
31a7(mdo sde): de nas grags 'dzin ma ci bdag la byang chub sems dpa' las gzhan su zhig khyer 'gyur snyam du bsams nas/ byang chub sems dpa'i thad du song ba dang / ji tsam
31a8(mdo sde): na gos dang rgyan thams cad byin zin nas ci yang ma lus pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' mgul na shun du mdzes shing rin che ba'i mu tig phreng cig lus pa
31b1(mdo sde): mthong nas de de la dga' ba bag bkum pa med rang nyid kyis bkrol te rang gi mgul du gtugs nas byang chub sems dpa'i thad nas song ste/ de nas rgyal po
31b2(mdo sde): zas gtsang ma 'di snyam du sems te/ bu mo 'di yid legs shing brtan pa las na gzhon nu thugs dang bsnun par nus kyis 'di blang bar bya'o snyam du bsams
31b3(mdo sde): nas/ grags 'dzin mi bu med kyi 'khor nyi khri dang / byang chub sems dpa'i btsun mor blangs so// rgyal po zas gtsang mas byang chub sems dpa'
31b4(mdo sde): la smras pa/ song las kyi mtha' ci tsam pa la ltos shig/ de nas byang chub sems dpa' rgyal po zas gtsang mas sgo ba bsan te/ shing tu bzang
31b5(mdo sde): po la zhugs nas phyi rol du gshegs te yab rgyal po zas gtsang ma'i las kyi mtha' gzigs shing / byang chub sems dpa'i las kyi mtha' la zhugs pa/
31b6(mdo sde): rnams kyi gam du byon pa dang / gshol lnga brgya dang zhing rmed cing zhing pa'i mi de rnams kyang gzhol gnod cing 'dren pas stobs nye bar nyams pa// mgo
31b7(mdo sde): lus rdul gyis g.yog pa dang / rlung dang than pas lus la brdungs pas lus rtsub cing mdog ngan pa/ rkang pa dang lag pa gas pa/ dengs shing /
31b8(mdo sde): dri ma can gyi gos gyon pa/ rkang pa dri ma can ltogs pa dang skom pas mdog ngan zhing lkog pa dang / mkhur ba dang mig gi logs skams pa dang /
32a1(mdo sde): glang de rnams kyang rmon pa lcags gzer bu rnon po can gyis lus bral bas brgya pa dang / 'jug mdo'i
32a2(mdo sde): phyogs khrag gis g.yogs pa/ ltogs pa dang skom pas dbugs rtsegs pa'i ring du 'dren la/ gnya' shing gis gnan pa'i rma las sna khrag 'dzag
32a3(mdo sde): pa la sbrang bu dang 'bu'i tshogs za ba mthong lcag kyis rkang pa rma byung zhing kha dang sna nas kha chu dang sna chu 'dzag la sbrang ma dang sha sbrang dang / sbrang bu mchu rings kyis yog
32a4(mdo sde): pa rnams gzigs so// gzigs nas kyang thog ma med pa'i dus nas bsod nams skyed cing / bsags pa'i thugs rjes kun nas bskyod pi thugs kyis zhing ba
32a5(mdo sde): rnams la 'di skad ces gsungs so// shes ldan dag khyed su yin de rnams kyis gsol pa/ byang chub sems dpa'i lag so// des gsungs pa/ shes ldan dag
32a6(mdo sde): khyed deng phan cad bran du mi bya/ mngag gzhugs par mi bya/ rang dbang can gar dga' bar 'gro bar byas/ bde ba la reg par gnas shig/ rmon pa rnams kyang bkrol
32a7(mdo sde): nas gsungs pa/ khyed cag kyang deng phan cad rtsa mchog ma nyams pa za zhing / chu ma brdul ma rnyog shing dngas pa dag la mthungs shig/ khyed la phyogs bzhi nas kyang
32a8(mdo sde): rlung bsil bar gyur cig/ de nas byang chub sems dpa' yid byung ba de nyid kyis/ yab zas gtsang gi bzhi blas kyi mtha' la gzigs nas/ snun zhing sngo la
32b1(mdo sde): grib
32b2(mdo sde): mdab ma thugs cing grib ma bzang po dang ldan pa'i 'dzam bu'i shing gi grib ma gang na ba der gshegs te byon nas shing 'dzam bu'i ma la bzhugs te/ 'dod pa las
32b3(mdo sde): dben pa'i sdig pa mi dge ba'i chos rnams las dben pa/ rtog pa dang bcas dpyod pa dang bcas shing / dben pa las skyes pa'i dga' dang bde ba zag pa med pa dang /
32b4(mdo sde): 'dra ba'i bsam gtan dang po la snyoms par zhugs so// skye bo tshogs chen po yid byang chub sems dpa' spangs te mi 'gro bar shing gzhan rnams kyi drung ni sdong ngo //
32b5(mdo sde): rgyal po zas gtsang gis bsams pa/ byang chub sems dpa' ring zhig thogs te/ da ltar dro'i dus las yol gyis ltar 'gro'i zhes de shing rtar zhugs nas zhing pa'i
32b6(mdo sde): grong du song ste/ phan tshun du byang chub sems dpa' tshol zhing shing 'dzam bu'i drung du phyin to// de'i tshe nyi ma'i gung yol nas shing gzhan rnams kyi grib ma shar phyogs su
32b7(mdo sde): gzhol/ shar phyogs su 'bab/ shar phyogs su bab par gyur to// byang chub sems dpa'i mthus 'dzam bu'i grib ma ni byang chub sems dpa'i sku mi gtod
32b8(mdo sde): ngo // rgyal po zas gtsang gis nyi mi'i gung yol nas shing gzhan rnams kyi grib ma ni shar phyogs su gzhol/ shar phyogasu 'bab/ shar phyogs su bab par gyur na shing
32b9(mdo sde): 'dzam bu'i grib ma ni byang chub sems dpa'i sku mi gtong ba mthong ngo // mthong nas kyang de 'di snyam du sems te/ gzhon nu ni rdzu 'phrul che zhing mthu che ba yin te/ 'di
33a1(mdo sde): mngon/ wAr de nyi ma'i gung yol nas shing gzhan rnams kyis grib ma ni shar phyogs su gzhol/ shar phyog su 'bab/ shar phyogasu bab par gyur na
33a2(mdo sde): shing 'dzam bu'i grib ma ni byang chub sems dpa'i sku mi gtong ba ngo mtshar che'o snyam mo// de nas dga' ba'i sti stang byas te/ byang chub sems dpa'i zhabs gnyis
33a3(mdo sde): la gtugs nas tshigs su bcas te smras pa/ ji ltar lham tshes ni g.yos pa ltar/ 'dzam bu'i grib ma khyod sku mi gtong ba/ blo chen khyod kyi ya mtshan gnyis 'di
