33a4(mdo sde): ste/ kun gzigs khyod kyi zhabs la phyag 'tshal lo// de nas byang chub sems dpa' ting nge 'dzin de las gzhengs nas shing rtar zhugs pa dang / ji tsam na gter
33a5(mdo sde): sbyong ba/ sgra dang kha spu dang ser mo ring ba gter thogs te byang chub sems dpa' gang na ba der song te phyin nas/ byang chub sems dpa' la 'di skad ces gsol/
33a6(mdo sde): to// lha gter 'di rnams bzhes shig/ byang chub sems dpas gsungs pa/ 'di gang gi lha skye bu gang zhig dus las 'das pa de rnams kyi lags so// byang
33a7(mdo sde): chub sems dpas gsungs pa/ 'di rnams kyis chog gis/ re zhig de rnams kyis blon po'i yongs su bzung ba byas nas ci zhig byas/ khyed nga la dgos pa
33a8(mdo sde): med kyis song shig/ tshigs su bcas pas gsungs pa/ gang gis nga la 'chi ba'i gtam smras pa/ de dag kyang shi gtam du gyur pa yin/ bdag
33b1(mdo sde): kyang shi nas ring po mi thogs par/ gzhan dag gi yang gtam du 'gyur b.ra'o// de rnams kyis yang sgra byung ba/ gzhon nu gal te mi bzhes na/ bdag cag rgya mtsho
33b2(mdo sde): chen por 'jug go// byang chub sems dpas ci bde bde bar zhugs shig ces gsungs pa dang / de rnams rgya mtsho chen po'i nang du bzhugs so// de nas gnas
33b3(mdo sde): gtsang ma'i ris lha rnams 'di snyam du sems te/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams ni rgyu'i stobs can yin mod kyi/ 'on kyang rkyen sgrub par bya dgongs te/ 'di ltar
33b4(mdo sde): rgyu'i stobs chen yang rkyen gyi stobs la ltos so snyam nas byang chub sems dpa' dur khrod kyi nang nas gshegs pa lha rnams kyis mi ro rnam par bsngos pa dang / rnam par
33b5(mdo sde): rnag pa dang / rnam par 'bus gzhigs pa dang / rnam par bam pa dang / rnam par zos pa zhig pa snyan pa dang / byang chub sems dpas gzigs nas skye ba 'khrud
33b6(mdo sde): so// de nas rgyal po zas gcad mas byang chub sems dpa' lam/ gzhan nas grong khyer ser skya'i bzhir 'jug par byas so// de nas grong khyer ser skya'i
33b7(mdo sde): bzhir bud med kyi tshogs skar khung dang skar khung dra ba can dang / ba gam dag na byang chub sems dpa' la lta zhing 'dug pa dang / shAkya dus legs kyi bu mo sa mam
33b8(mdo sde): ma zhes bya ba steng gi khang bzangs kyi bzhi la 'dug pa/ byang chub sems dpa' la rtog pa na/ rkang pa'i mthe bos sa la bskos te khrag byung ba yang ma mtshor ro//
34a1(mdo sde): byang chub sems dpa' yang sa mcho ma la gzigs pa na phyag g.yas kyi mda' phye mar grags so// kha lo bas lcags mda' phul ba
34a2(mdo sde): dang / de yang bye mar grags so// de nas rgyal po zas gtsang ma 'di snyam du sems te/ 'dis ni gzhon nu'i thugs dang sbun par nus so snyams mo// de nas kha la
34a3(mdo sde): sgyur bas shing rta drangs pa dang / shAkya dril bu'i sgra'i bu mo ri dwags skyes shes bya bas byang chub sems dpa' shing rtar zhugs te byon pa mthong ba dang / yang steng gi khang
34a4(mdo sde): bzangs kyi gzhi la 'dug nas/ tshigs su bcad de smras pa/ kye ma 'di'i yum bde zhing yab kyang shing du bde ba yin/ kye ma gang gi khyim thab gyur/
34a5(mdo sde): bud med de yang mya ngan 'das/ skyes mchog bsams gtan pa de yis/ mya ngan 'das pa'i sgra gsan nas/ mya ngan 'das pa zhi nyid du/ mkhyen nas de las
34a6(mdo sde): thugs dges gyur/ de nas byang chub sems dpa' mya ngan las 'das pa'i sgra gsan pas ri dgas skyes la dgyes te/ mgul nas mu tig phreng cig phog ste/
34a7(mdo sde): 'phangs nas shing rta de la bsam gtan la snyoms par 'jug zhugs par mdzad do// phreng ba de yang de'i mgul du kris par gyur to// de nas rgyal po zas gtsang ma

34b1(mdo sde): kyang bung med nyi khris bskor ba byang chub sems dpa'i btsun mo blangs so// de ltar grags 'dzin ma dang / sa mtsho ma dang / ri dgas skyes la sogs pa btsun/

34b7(mdo sde): mos tshal gyi gzhir gshegs bzhed par gyur pa'i tshe/ kha lo sgyur ba la kye kha lo sgyur ba re shig bzhon pa bzang po myur ba shoms shig dang der zhugs nas

35a1(mdo sde): mngon/ shig bzhon pa bzang po myur du shoms shig dang / der zhugs nas bskyed mos tshal gyi bzhir 'gro'o// lha bka' bzhin 'anal
35a2(mdo sde): zhes kha lo sgyur ba byang chub sems dpa' shAkya thub pa'i ltar mnyan nas/ gzhon pa bzang po myur du bshams te/ byang chub sems dpa' shAkya thub pa gang na ba der song

36a1(mdo sde): mngon/ @/ sgyur ba mi rgas 'khogs gtugs pa phyam dgu'o ltar kyar kyor can mdun nas 'khar ba la rten cing lus 'dar zhing 'gro la de'i sgra ser

36b1(mdo sde): par rab tu 'byung bar 'gyur du 'ong gis/ ma la bdag gis gzhon nu la 'dod pa'i yon tan lnga las phal po che zhig byin la/ ci nas kyang 'di la dga' zhing rab tu 'byung

36b6(mdo sde): gsung bar 'gyur bas/ de nas byang chub sems dpas kho lo sgyur ba las gsungs pa/ kye kha lo sgyur ba re shig gzhon pa bzang po myur du shoms shig dang / de la
36b7(mdo sde): da zhon nas bskyed mos tshal gyi bzhir gshegs so// lha bka' bzhin tshal zhes kha lo sgyur bas byang chub sems dpa' shAkya thub pa'i ltar mnyan nas zhon pa bzang
36b8(mdo sde): po bshams te/ byang chub sems dpa' shAkya thub pa gang na ba der song ste phyin nas/ byang chub sems dpa' shAkya thub pa la 'di skad ces gsol to// byang chub
37a1(mdo sde): mngonasems dpa' shAkya thub pas mi skye bo zab por rid pa nyam rung ba dbang po nyams pa/ skye bo mang po'i mig gis lha mi phod pa zhig
37a2(mdo sde): gzigaso// gzigs nas kyang kha lo sgyur ba la gsungs pa/ kha lo sgyur ba mi skya rbab rbab po ring pa nyam chung ba dbang po nyams pa skye bo mang po'i mig gi wA
37a3(mdo sde): mi phod pa 'di ci yin/ lha 'di ni bro nad kyis thebs pa zhes bgyi'o// kha lo sgyur ba nad kyis thebs pa zhes bya ba 'di ci yin/ lha mi 'di gang gis 'gum par

39a1(mdo sde): don/ mtshungs pa/ 'dod pa'i yon tan lnga pos kun dges pa/ mig stong dga' ba'i tshul na gnas pa bzhin/ de nas gnas gtsang ma'i ris//

51a5(mdo sde): de bas na bdag cag rnams sangs rgyas kyi zhing du gnas par mi nus pas na/ bdag cag yongs su mya ngan las 'da'o// sha na'i gos 'di zas cang
51a6(mdo sde): ma'i sras la khye kyis phul cig/ bdag nyid chen po de ni bla na med pa'i ye shes thugs su chud par 'gyur la/ khyed kyi kyang 'bras bu chen po thob par
51a7(mdo sde): 'gyur ro// zhes smras nas 'bar ba dang / gsal ba dang / char 'phebs pa dang / klog 'byin pa'i cho 'phrul dag byas nas/ phung po lhag med pa'i
51a8(mdo sde): mya ngan las pa'i dbyings su mya ngan las 'das so// rgan mo des kyang 'chi kar gos de dag bu mo la gtad nas ji ltar 'gyur pa rnams smras so// de'i bu
51b1(mdo sde): yang nad kyis thebs te 'chi bar shes nas/ des kyang shing drung gcig tu gzhag nas/ shing de la gnas pa'i lha gang yin pa de la/ khyed kyis
51b2(mdo sde): 'di dag rgyal po zas gtsang gis sras la phu kha cig ces gsol ba btab po// lha rnams kyi dbang po rgya byin gyis shes pa mthong ba ni/ 'og tu 'jug
51b3(mdo sde): pa yin pas de dag shes nas blangs te/ de nas rngon pa rgas 'khogs pa lta bu zhig tu bdag nyid mngon par sprul nas/ de dag dgongs te lag pa la
51b4(mdo sde): mnga' zhu thogs byang chub sems dpa' gshegs pa'i lam kar ldang ba dang / byang chub sems dpa' yang rim gyis lam der byon nas/ rngon pa lag
51b5(mdo sde): na mda' zhu thogs shing gos dur mrig gyon pa zhig gzigs so// gzigs nas kyang mi de la gzigs pa/ kA'i nang rje sha na'i gos so ni dag ni rab tu
51b6(mdo sde): byung ba la mtsham pa yin gyi/ ka shi ka'i ras phran 'di dag khyed la 'o ni dag nga la byin cig/ des gsol pa/ gzhon nu bdag la gzhan dag khyod kyis
51b7(mdo sde): rgyal bu gzhon nu grongs nas ka shi ka'i ras phran gyis gos 'di dag blangs so zhes bzhi de yar 'chi bar 'gyur lags pas/ bdag 'di dag mi 'bul lo//
51b8(mdo sde): byang chub sems dpas gsungs pa/ kye nang rje ni mthu' ji lta bu dang ldan pa 'jig rten thams cad kyis shes te/ su zhig gis dgrongs par nus/ khyed kyis
52a1(mdo sde): nga 'grongs par su zhig yid ches kyis bag tsha ba med par byin cig/ de nas lha rnams kyi dbang po brgya byin gyis byang chub sems dpa'i zhabs gnyis
52a2(mdo sde): la gtugs nas sha na'i gos dag phul te/ ka shi ka'i ras phran rnams blangs so// byang chub sems dpa'i sku dang sha ni'i gos dag 'tsham par ma gyur pa dang /
52a3(mdo sde): dang / de 'di snyam du dgongs te/ kye ma 'o sha na'i gos rnams bdag gi sku dang / mtsham par gyur cig snyam nas tshigs smras ma thag tu/ sha na'i gos de dag 'di
52a4(mdo sde): ltar byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi byang chub sems dpa'i mthu dang / lha rnams kyi'i lha'i mthus byang chub sems dpa'i sku dang mtshams par gyur to// de nas
52a5(mdo sde): byang chub sems dpa' 'di snyam dgongs te/ da ni bdag rab tu byung zin gyis 'gro ba rnams rjes su bzung bar bya'o snyam mo// de nas byang chub sems dpa'
52a6(mdo sde): mthar kyis rgyu zhing gshegs pa dang / rgyal po'i khab du byon to// byang chub sems dpa' gzo'i gnas dang las kyi gnas de dang de rnams la mkhas pa yin
52a7(mdo sde): pas des shing ka ra bi ra'i lo ma las lhung bzed byas spyod lam zhibs rgyal po'i khab tu bsod snyoms kyi phyir zhugs so// de'i tshe rgyal po gzugs can snying po
52a8(mdo sde): steng gi khang bzangs kyi bzhir 'dug pa des 'gro ba dang / ldog pa dang / lta ba dang / rnam par lta ba dang / bskum pa dang / brkyang ba dang / chos gos snam sbyar
52b1(mdo sde): dang / lhung bzed thogs pa mdzes pas bsod snyoms spyod pa mthong ngo // mthong nas kyang 'di snyam du sems te/ rgyal po khab nas rab tu byung ba ji snyed cig gnas/
52b2(mdo sde): pa la rab tu byung ba 'di'i spyod lam de lta bu ni mga' yang med do snyam mo// 'dir smras pa/ ji ltar mig can 'gro ba ltar/ rab tu byung ba spags par bya/
52b3(mdo sde): 'di na rtag par mdzad nas su/ rab tu byung ba yang dag bzhed/ khyim nas 'di ni sdug bsngal te/ 'di ni rdul gri gnas yin zhing / rab tu byung bar snang ltar/
52b4(mdo sde): mkhyen nas de'i tshe rab tu byung / rab tu byung nas sku yis ni/ sdig pa'i las ni spangs pa dang / gsung gi sdig pa spangs pa ni/ 'tshe ba kun nas dag par/
52b5(mdo sde): mdzad/ de nas ma ga da'i ni/ grong mchog rgyal po'i khab gshegs nas/ mgon po shes bzhin dran ldan pa/ bsod pasnyoms phyirani gshegs pa
52b6(mdo sde): pa der/ bzod sbyangs ma ga de'i bdag / khang bzangs la ni 'dug pas mthong / mthong nas sems dad de nas ni/ blon po rnams la 'di skad smras/ mtsham
52b7(mdo sde): gis ni rgyas gyur cig/ kho lag phun sum tshogs pa dang / mnya' shing gang du lta ba'i/ 'di ye shes ldan dag ltos shig/ spun mi brdeg la yid
52b8(mdo sde): bzhungs shing / dman pa'i rigs las mkhrungs 'di/ gang du gnas par gshegs 'gyur ba/ rgyal pos pa nye rjes bzhin btang de nas po nya la sgob/
53a1(mdo sde): mngonadage sbyong de ni gar 'gro zhing / gang du gnas ni btab pa'i/ rjes bzhin du ni 'brang bar gyis/ des ni bsod snyom gshegs

53a5(mdo sde): seng ge'am stag gi phru gu dang / ri sul dag na gnas pa ltar/ brgyab seng gi ni steng na gnas/ pho nya rnams kyis tshigs thos nas/ sa bdag
53a6(mdo sde): shing drung zhugs gnas ni/ de ni blon pos yongs bskor nas/ myur ba kho nar dong bar gyur// bzhon pas bzod pa'i sar zhon te/ de ni zhon pa
53a7(mdo sde): pa la babs nas/ rkang gis nye bar song nas ni/ de nas de bzhin gshegs pa mthong / rgyal po 'dug nas dgyes pa dang / mgu bar 'gyur ba'i
53a8(mdo sde): gtam gsol nas/ de ni ma khengs mi blang bar/ don 'di dag ni rab smras so// dge slong lang tse dang po la/ bab par yang dag gnas gyur
53b1(mdo sde): cing / 'di 'drar gi za brjid ldan pa la/ bsod snyoms spyod pa brjes ma lags/ khang pa nyams dga' dag dang ni/ bud med rgyan gyis brgyan pa dang / longs
53b2(mdo sde): spyod mchog ni khyod gsol na/ nyid kyi gdung ni zhu yis gsungs/ rgyal po gangs ri nye ba na/ yul gyi ljongs ni nor dag dang / 'bru dag gis ni gang gyur
53b3(mdo sde): pa/ ko sa la zhes grags pa yod/ bu ra ma shing pa nyi ma'i rus/ shAkya dag ni de na gnas/ rgyal po nga'i rgyal rigs te/ nga ni 'dod pa'i don mi
53b4(mdo sde): gnyer/ sa 'di ri dang bcas shing rgya mtsho la bcas/ rin chen kun dang ldan pa 'byor gyur kyang / mi ni nams kyang ngom par mi 'gyur te/ so gas dus
53b5(mdo sde): shing gi mi bzhin no// 'dod pa rnams ni sha kho na 'brel/ ces gsungs/ mi dbang rgal bar dka' zhing 'dam rdzab 'dra// sdug bsngal dang ni mya ngan
53b6(mdo sde): 'jigs pa yi/ brtsa ba'i gartso ste blo ngan rnams kyis bsten/ rgyal po ngas ni byung ma thag tu yang / 'dod pa rnams la mi dga'i blo bskyed na/ 'jigs
53b7(mdo sde): byed chos kyi dgra bor gyur pa dag bor ba de kho slar yang ci ltar blang / rtse mo sna tshogs yangs par gyur pa'i/ lhun po gangs can rlung gis bskyod srid
53b8(mdo sde): kyinga'i blo ni thar pa dang / 'dod pa'i shugs kyis bskyod par mi nus so// 'jig rten 'di na 'dod par byeng gyur nas/ 'khor ba'i
54a1(mdo sde): dona'akhor los yongs su 'khyam pa la/ mi dbang sgrubs te gzhan pa na/ 'jigs pa che las de ni thar bar byed/ 'dod pa
54a2(mdo sde): rnams kyis nyes dmigs mkhyen/ mya ngan 'das pa zhi ba gzigs/ spang phyir gang du nga'i yid/ dag pa dag tu 'gro bar bya/ rgyal po gzugs can
54a3(mdo sde): snying pos gsol ba/ kye rab tu byung ba cul zhugs ji zhig don du gnyer/ des gsungs pa/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub bo//
54a4(mdo sde): rgyal pos gsol pa/ kye rab tu byung ba gang gi tshe khyod bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngon par sangs rgyas par 'gyur ba de'i tshe bdag la

54a8(mdo sde): gal te de rnams gdung ba lnga'i sbyor bas nyin thun cig 'dug pa de'i tshe byang chub sems dpas kyang sbyor ba des thun gnyis su zhugs so//
54b1(mdo sde): nas de rnams ya mtshan skyes nas dge sbyong 'di ni/ chen po zhig go zhes smras pas/ dge sbyong chen po zhes bya bar 'gyur to// byang chub sems
54b2(mdo sde): dpas de rnams la smras pa/ shes ldan dag khyed rtul zhugs 'dis ci zhig don du gnyer/ de nas kha cig gis gsol pa/ brgya byin nyid do//
54b3(mdo sde): kha cig gis gsol pa/ bdag nyid ni tshangs pa nyid do// kha cig gis gsol pa/ bdag cag ni bdud ngo // byang chub sems dpas
54b4(mdo sde): dgongs pa/ drang srong 'di dag ni slar yang ltung ba/ lam 'di ni shes par nus pa ma yin/ mthong bar nus pa ma yin/ bla na med pa yang dag
54b5(mdo sde): par rdzogs pa'i byang chub par nus pa ma yin no// de nas byang chub sems dpas lam de nyid nus pa med par mkhyen nas/ sgyu rtsal shes kyi bu ring 'phur
54b6(mdo sde): gang na ba der gshegs te byon pa dang / sgyu rtsal shes kyi bu ring 'phur la 'di skad ces gsungs so// ring 'phur gal te khyod la mi bde med na khyod kyi drung du
54b7(mdo sde): kho bo tshangs pa spyod pa spyad do// des smras pa/ tshe dang ldan pa ko'u ta ma bdag la mi bde ba med kyis/ ci bde ba kho nar bzhugs shig/ byang

55a1(mdo sde): don/ tshe dang ldan pa ko'u ta ma ci yang med pa'i skye mched kyi bar du'o// de nas byang chub sems dpa' 'di snyam du dgongs te/

55a3(mdo sde): la yang brtson 'grus dang dran pa dang / ting nge 'dzin dang / shes rab yod pas sgyu rtsal shes kyi bu ring 'phur gyis ci yang med pa'i skye mched kyi bar gyi chos de

55a5(mdo sde): pa thob par bya ba'i phyir dang / ma rtogs pa rtogs par bya ba'i phyir dang / mngon sum du ma byas pa mngon sum du byas pa'i phyir dang / gcig pu dben pa

55a8(mdo sde): 'phur gang na ba der gshegs te/ byon nas sgyu rtsa la shes kyi bu ring 'phur 'di skad ces gsungs so// ring 'phur khyod kyis ci yang med pa'i skye mched
55b1(mdo sde): kyi bar gyi chos 'di dag rang gi mngon par shes pas mngon sum du byas sam/ des 'di skad ces smras so// tshe dang ldan pa ko'u ta ma med de bdag gis ci yang med/

55b3(mdo sde): kyi bar gyi chos de dag rang mngon par shes pas mngon sum du byas so// tshe dang ldan pa ko'u ta ma de ltar na khod ci tsam pa bdag gi yang de tsam la/ bdag gi ji tsam
55b4(mdo sde): pa khyod kyi yang de tsam pas don 'di la 'o skol mtshungs shing mnyam ste 'dra bar thob kyis tshur spyon 'o skol gnyis gis 'khor 'di yongs su dran par bgyi'o// de nas sgyu

55b7(mdo sde): nus pa ma yin/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub par nus pa ma yin no snyam mo// de nas byang chub sems dpas lam de nus pa med par rigs
55b8(mdo sde): nas/ rangs byed kyi bu lhag spyod gang na ba der gshegs te byon nas/ rangs byed kyi bu lhag spyod la 'di skad ces gsungs so// lhag spyod gal te khyod la/
56a1(mdo sde): don/ mi bde ba med na/ khyod kyi drung du tshangs par spyod pa spyad do// nges gsol pa/ tshed dang ldan klo'u ta ma bdag la mi bde

56a6(mdo sde): de rnams kho na ma thob par bya ba'i phyir dang / ma rtogs pa rtogs par bya ba'i phyir dang / mngon sum du ma byas pa mngon sum du bya ba'i phyir dang / gcig pu
56a7(mdo sde): dben pa/ bag yod pa/ rtun pa dang ldan pa/ bdag nyid gtod par gnas te/ gcig pu dper par bag yod pa bdag nyid gtod par gnas pa na/

56b6(mdo sde): de nas rangs byed kyi bu lhag spyod byang chub sems da pa'i thog ma'i slob dpon gyis byang chub sems dpa' la brjed pa dam pas brjed cing mchod pas mchod do//

57a3(mdo sde): srungs kyi sde'i grong rdal gang na ba der rgyu zhing gshegs te byon nas de phan tshun 'chad pa na/ phyogs dga' ltar 'dug pa/ nags tshang tshing mdzes pa/ chu klung ne ran dza
57a4(mdo sde): na bsil bar 'bab pa/ gse gu can 'jug dog bde zhing mtha' che la gsing ma sngon po dang / shing sna tshogs kyis rgyan pa dga' ltar 'dug pa zhig gzigs so//

57a8(mdo sde): bya'o snyam mo// de nas byang chub sems dpa' nags du zhugs te shing gi drung du bzhugs nas tshems la tshems gtad/ ljags da ka na la ba car na thugs kyi
57b1(mdo sde): thugs mngon du bzung / mngon du bsdams/ shin du mngon du bsdams so// de thugs kyis thugs mngon du bzung / mngon du bsdams/ shing du mngon du bsdum
57b2(mdo sde): pas/ ba spu'i khung bu thams cad nas rdul byung bar gyur te/ dper na mi stobs dang ldan pas mi stobs dang ldan pas mi stobs shin du chung ba zhig phyi ka log du bzung /
57b3(mdo sde): mngon du bsdams/ shin du mngon du bsdams na de'i ba spu'i khung bu thams cad nas rdul byung ba de bzhin du de'i tshe/ byang chub sems dpa' tshems la tshems gtang
57b4(mdo sde): ljags bkan la bcar te/ thugs kyis thugs mngon du bzung / mngon du bsdams/ shin du mngon du bsdams pa la sogs pa ni snga ma bzhin no// de nas byang chub

57b6(mdo sde): bsam gtan dag la snyoms par zhugs pa na zhal dang / shang nas dbugs rngub pa dang 'byung ba 'gags so// de'i zhal dang shangs nas dbugs rngub pa dang
57b7(mdo sde): 'byung ba 'gags pa na rlung thams cad spyi bo'i nang du du song nas de'i dbu la dbu'i tshor ba shin du mi bzad pa skyes so// dper na mi stobs dang ldan pas mi stobs
57b8(mdo sde): shin du chung ba'i spyi bor lcags kyi phur pa sngon pos btab na/ de'i mgo la mgo'i tshor ba shin du mi bzad pa skye ba de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' rnams par 'am
58a1(mdo sde): pa'i bsam gtan dag la snyoms par zhugs na/ dbu la dbu'i tshor ba shin du mi bzad pa skyes kyang de zhum pa ma yin gyi brtson
58a2(mdo sde): 'grus brtsams pa yin sku spungs pa ma yin gyi ma sbyangs pa ma yin/ rmugs pa ma yin gyi dran pa nye bar bzhag pa yin te/ sems gcig tu mnyam par bzhag pa
58a3(mdo sde): yin no// byang chub sems dpa' sdug bsngal drag po mi bzad pa rtsa ba pa tsha ba yid du mi 'ong ba'i tshor ba de lta bu nyams su myong yang 'di ltar sku sgoms pa yin pa'i phyir

85a6(mdo sde): de nas de yi som nyi thams cad 'bral/ gang tshe chos 'di dag ni skyed pa'i/ brtson 'grus ldan pa'i bsam gtan tshangs pa yin/ 'jig rten kun
85a7(mdo sde): du snang bar 'dug pa ni/ ji ltar bar snang nyi ma shar ba bzhin/ gang tshe chos 'di dag ni skyed byed pa'i/ brtson 'grus ldan pa'i bsam gtan
85a8(mdo sde): tshangs pa 'di/ bdud kyi sde rnam par bcom gnas te/ sangs rgyas kun du sbyor las rnam par grol/ de nas bcom ldan 'das 'di snyam du
85b1(mdo sde): dgongs te/ bdag gi chos zab mo zab par dka' zhing khong du chud par dka' ba/ rtog ge ba rnams kyi rtog ge ba'i spyod yul ma yin pa ste/
85b2(mdo sde): zhing mo 'dzangs pa'i mkhas pa dang / rig pas rnam par shes par bya ba togs te/ de bdag gis gzhan la smras kyang gzhan gyis de shes pas nges
85b3(mdo sde): bdag dub par 'gyur/ ngal bar 'gyur/ sems la spro ba med pa kho nar 'gyur bar zad pas/ ma la bdag gcag gcig pu dgon pa'i nags
85b4(mdo sde): stug por mthong ba'i chos la bde bar gnas pa'i rnal 'byor la rjes su brtson par bya'o snyam ste/ de nas bcom ldan 'das thugs las chung ngus
85b5(mdo sde): bzhugs pa las thugs gzhol ba mdzad cing / chos 'chad pa la ma yin no// de nas tshengs pa mi mdzad kyi bdag po 'di snyam du sems te/

85b7(mdo sde): bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas 'jig rten 'byung ba ni/ dper na u dum pa ri me tog bzhin no// bcom ldan 'das de da ltar

86a2(mdo sde): brkum nas brkyang ba 'am/ brkyang nas brkums pa tsam gyis tshangs pa'i mi mjed kyi bdag tshangs pa'i 'jig rten nas mi snang bar byas te/ bcom ldan
86a3(mdo sde): 'das kyi spyan sngar 'dug go// de nas tshangs pa mi mjed kyi bdag pos/ de'i tshe tshigs su bcad de gsol pa/ ma ga dang ni sngon cad chos 'byung na/ dag
86a4(mdo sde): pa ma lags dri mar bcas pas rtogs/ bdud rtsi chos kyi sgo ni phye mdzod la/ dri ma med pas rtogs pa bshad par mdzod/ de nas bcom ldan 'das
86a5(mdo sde): kyis de'i tshe tshigs su bcad de bka' stsal pa/ tshangs pa ngas ni tshogs chen gyis/ skyon rnams bcom nas rtogs gyur pa/ srid dang chags pas bkris
86a6(mdo sde): rnams kyis/ chos 'di legs par rtogs mi 'gyur/ rgyun las zlog phyogs 'gro ba'i lam/ zab cing shin du mthong dka' ba/ mun pa'i phung po sgrib
86a7(mdo sde): pa yis/ 'dod chags zhen pas mthong mi 'gyur/ btsun pa 'jig rten du skyes shing 'jig rten du rgas pa'i sems can rnams la dbang po rnon po dang /
86a8(mdo sde): dbang po 'bring po dang / dbang po rtul po dang / drang sla ba dang / gdul sla ba dang / nyon mongs pa chung ba'i rigs mchis te/ de dag gis dam pa'i

86b2(mdo sde): por 'gyur te/ chab nas 'phags te kha cig ni chab kyi nang du nub cing mchis pa de bzhin du/ btsun pa 'jig rten du skyes shing 'jig rten du rgas pa'i sems can
86b3(mdo sde): rnams la yang dbang po rnon po dang / dbang po 'bring po// dbang po rtul po dang / drang sla ba dang / gdul sla ba dang / nyon mongs pa chung ba dang / rdul chung
86b4(mdo sde): ba'i rigs mchis te/ de dag gis dam pa'i chos ma thos na yongs su nyams par 'gyur bas/ chos rin po che 'tshal bar 'gyur ba mchis kyis/ bcom ldan
86b5(mdo sde): 'das kyis bsha du gsol/ bde bar gshegs pa chos bshad du gsol/ de nas bcom ldan 'das 'di snyam du dgongs te/ ma la nga nyid kyi sangs rgyas kyi sman
86b6(mdo sde): gyi 'jig rten la blta bar bya'o snyam nas/ de nas bcom ldan 'das nyid kyi sangs rgyas kyi spyan gyis 'jig rten la gzigs te/ bcom ldan 'das sangs rgyas

87a3(mdo sde): pa mi rnams la ni gya nom chos/ glan ka mi btsal mdo tsam bshad par bya/ de nas tshangs pa mi mjed kyi bdag po 'di snyam du sems te/ kye bcom ldan 'das kyis chos
87a4(mdo sde): bshad par 'gyur ro// kye bde bar gshegs pas chos bstan par 'gyur ro snyam du rig nas/ dga' ba dang / mgu ba dang / mchod tu dga' ba dang / dga'

87a6(mdo sde): snang gyur to// de nas bcom ldan 'das 'di snyam du dgongs to// ngas su la thog mar chos bshad par bya snyam mo// de nas bcom ldan 'das 'di snyam du dgongs te/

87a8(mdo sde): dam pas mchod la/ rtogs pa dam pa dag la yid rangs shing dad par 'gyur pa yin no snyam mo// bcom ldan 'das lha rnams kyis gsol pa/ brdzun pa sgyu rtsal shes
87b1(mdo sde): kyi bu gum nas rlung bdun lon lags so// bcom ldan 'das kyis kyang dgongs pa la bzhugs te ye shes gzigs pa sgyu rtsal shes kyi bu ring pur shi nas zhag bdun
87b2(mdo sde): no// de nas bcom ldan 'das 'di snyam du dgongs te/ e ma 'o sgyu rtsal shes kyi bu ring phur shi ba de ni te bor ma stes so// e ma'o sgyu rtsal shes kyi bu ring phur ba de ni
87b3(mdo sde): shin du te bor ma stes so// chos 'dul ba 'di thos ma thos so// gal te 'dis chos 'dul ba thos na shes par 'gyur ba zhig snyam mo// de nas bcom ldan 'das 'di
87b4(mdo sde): snyam du dgongs te/ ma la nges thog mar su zhig la chos bshad snyam mo// de nas bcom ldan 'das 'di snyam du dgongs te/ me la ngas rangs byed kyi bu lhag spyod de
87b5(mdo sde): la thog mar chos bshad par bya ste/ de ni nga'i thog pa'i slob dpon kho na yid bzhin du brjed pa'i dam pas brjed cing mchod pa'i dam pas brjed cing mchod pa'i dam pas

87b7(mdo sde): spyod ma dang gsum srod la gum lags so// bcom ldan 'das kyis dgongs pa las zhus te ye shes gzigs pa skyed na rangs byed kyi bu lhag spyod shi bar gyur to// de
87b8(mdo sde): nas bcom ldan 'das 'di snyam du dgongs te/ e ma'o rangs byed kyi bu lhag spyong shi ba de ni nye bor ma skyes so// e ma'o rangs byed kyi bu lhag spyod shi ba ni shin du te
88a1(mdo sde): bor ma stes so// chos 'dul ba 'di ma thos so// gal te nges chos 'dul ba 'di thos na shes par 'gyur ba zhig snga mo//

92a1(mdo sde): rabacas pa'i 'jig rten du bdud dang tshangs pa dang bcas/ dge slong dang bram zer bcas pa'i skye dgu dang mir bcas 'di las grog

112b2(mdo sde): 'di skad ces gsol to// dge sbyong chen po byon tam/ nas 'di snyam du gal te ma ga ta'i mi rnams kyis dge sbyong chen po ni 'di ltar rdzu 'phrul che ba mthu che ba

112b4(mdo sde): zhig 'di nas gzhan du song yang ci ma rung snyam sems pa ma yin nam/ nga'i thugs kyis khyod kyi sems shes nas zhag bdun nas gzhan du song ngo // 'o na
112b5(mdo sde): ci'i slad du 'dir byon lags/ 'od srung khyod kyi mchod sbyin zhag bdun byas zan nas 'di snyam du bdag la zhag bdun du rnyed pa dang / bkur sti chen po byung
112b6(mdo sde): zhing bza' ba dang / bca' ba rab tu mang po dang yang dbang du gyur gyis/ kye ma dge sbyong chen po 'ongs kyang ci ma rung / bdag gis de yang de la yongasu
112b7(mdo sde): longs spyod du bzhug go snyam du sems pa ma yin nas/ dge sbyong chen po de lta lagaso// nga'i thugs kyis khyod kyi sems shes nas nga 'ongs pa yin no//
112b8(mdo sde): dge sbyong chen po ci ba de kho nar longs spyod du gsol/ de nas lteng rgyas 'od srung ral pa can 'di snyam du sems te/ 'di ltar dge sbyong chen po rdzu 'phrul
112b9(mdo sde): che zhing thu che ba yin te/ ya mtshan chen mod kyi bdag kyang dgra bcom pa yin no snyam mo// de nas lteng rgyas 'od srung ral pa can gyis bcom ldan 'das
112b10(mdo sde): ldan pa skye bo'i tshogs chen po

113a3(mdo sde): 'od srung ral pa gyis bcom ldan 'das kyis ched du rang kho nas g.yos byas nas/ bcom ldan 'das gang na ba der song ste phyin nas/ bcom ldan 'das

113a6(mdo sde): mnyam par bzhag nas/ shing 'dzam bu zhes bya ba gang gis 'dzam bu'i gling du gdags pa de las kha dog dang / dri dang ro dang ldan pa'i 'dzam bu'i snye ma rnams
113a7(mdo sde): kyis lhung bzed bkang nas bsnams te/ lteng rgyas 'od bsrung ral pa can gyi bsti gnas gang na ba der gshegs pa de lta bu'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs
113a8(mdo sde): te/ byon nas bdan bsham pa nyid la bzhugs so// de nas de'i 'og tu lteng rgyas 'od srung ral pa can 'ongs nas/ lteng rgyas 'od srung ral pa can gyis bcom
113b1(mdo sde): ldan 'das bsti gnas kyi bdan bshams pa nyid la bzhugs pa mthong ngo // mthong nas 'di skad ces gsol to// dge sbyong chen po byon tam/ 'od srung

113b3(mdo sde): gzhag nas shing 'dzam bu zhes bya ba gang gis 'dzam bu'i gling du bdags bde las kha dog dang dri dang ro dang ldan pa'i 'dzam bu'i snyem rnams kyis lhung bzed bkang nas
113b4(mdo sde): 'dir phyin pa 'di lta bu'i ting nge 'dzin la snyom par zhugs kyis/ gal te 'dod na spyod cig/ dge sbyong chen po ci bde kho nar tshal lags so// de nas lteng
113b5(mdo sde): rgyas 'od bsrung ral pa can 'di snyam du sems te/ 'di ltar dge sbyong chen po rdzu 'phrul che zhing mthu che ba yin te/ ya mtshan chen mod kyi bdag kyang dgra bcom
113b6(mdo sde): pa yin no snyam mo// shing 'dzam bu zhes bya ba gang gi 'dzam bu'i gling du bdags pa de dang ha cang mi ring ba zhig na/ a ru'i nags dang / bil ba'i nags
113b7(mdo sde): dang / ki pad tha'i nags dang / skyu ru ra'i nags kyang de bzhin no// byang gi sgra mi snyan gyi gling du gshegs nas ma rmos ma btab pa'i 'bras sa lu lhung bzed
113b8(mdo sde): bkang ste bsnams nas/ lteng rgyas 'od srung ral pa can gyi bsti gnas gang na ba der gshegs te byon nas/ bdan bshams pa nyid la bzhugs so// de nas
114a1(mdo sde): 'das

114a3(mdo sde): pa nyid la bzhugs pa mthong ngo // mthong nas kyang 'di skad ces gsol to// dge slong chen po byon tam/ 'od srung 'ong so// dge sbyong chen po khyod kyi lhung bzed

114a5(mdo sde): pa btab pa'i 'bras sa lu'i 'bras lhung blakang nas/ 'dir phyin pa de lta bu'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs kyis/ gal nye 'dod na longs spyod cig/ dge
114a6(mdo sde): spong chen po ci bde kho nar 'tshal lags so// de nas lteng rgyas 'od bsrung ral pa can 'di snyam du sems te/ 'di ltar dge slong chen po rdzu 'phrul che zhing mthu
114a7(mdo sde): che ba yin te/ ya mtshan che mod kyi bdag kyang dgra bcom pa yin no snyam mo// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis lteng rgyas 'od srung ral pa can las bsod snyoms
114a8(mdo sde): bzhes nas/ phyogs gzhan zhig du bzhugs nas zhal zas kyi bya ba mdzad do// de nas bcom ldan 'das la chus chu'i dgongs pa zhig byung ngo // de nas lha'i
114a9(mdo sde): dbang po brgya byin gyis bcom ldan 'das la nus chu'i dgongs pa byung bar shes nas/ bcom ldan 'das gang na ba der song ste phyin nas bcom ldan 'das kyi spyan
114b1(mdo sde): mdor lags pas sa la bsnun pa dang / de nas bkod po zhig byung ste/ chu bab pa de la bcom ldan 'das kyis chus chu'i bya ba mdzad do// lteng rgyas 'od
114b2(mdo sde): srung ral pa can bsti gnas na 'chags pa na bkod pa byung ste chu 'bab pa mthong ngo // mthong nas kyang 'di snyam du sems te/ chu 'di sngon ni med na chu 'di da
114b3(mdo sde): ltar gang nas 'bab snyam mo// de nas lteng rgyas 'od bsrung ral pa can bcom ldan 'das gang na ba der song ste phyin nas/ bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces
114b4(mdo sde): gsol to// dge sbyong chen po mkhyen par mdzad du gsol/ bdag 'dir bsti gnas 'chag pa na bkod po'i chab cig mthong ngo // mthong nas kyang bdag
114b5(mdo sde): 'di snyam du sems te/ chu 'di sngon ma mchis na/ da ltar chu 'di gang nas 'bab snyam bgyid do// 'od srung 'dir khyod las bsod snyoms bzhes nas/
114b6(mdo sde): phyogs 'dir bzhugs te zhal zas kyi bya ba mdzad pa na/ nga la chus chu'i dgongs pa zhig byung ngo // de nas lha rnams kyi dbang po brgya byin gyis nga la chus
114b7(mdo sde): chu'i dgongs pa byung bar shes nas/ nga gang na der 'ongs te phyin nas/ nga'i mdun du lag pas sa la bsnun pa las sa las bsnun pa las de nas bkod
114b8(mdo sde): pa chen po zhig byung ba la ngas chus chu'i bya ba mdzad de/ 'od srung rdzing 'di ni lag pas rkos pa zhes pa zhes bya'o// de nas lteng rgyas 'od srung ral pa can 'di
115a1(mdo sde): na snyam du sems 'di skar dge srung chen po rdzu 'phrul che zhing mthu che ba yin te/ ya mtshan che mod kyi bdag kyang dam bcom pa yin na
115a2(mdo sde): snyam po// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyi 'bring du yang dag 'jom las gzhengs nas/ dzing lag pas rkos pa de gang na ba der gshegs te byon nas/ rdzing lag
115a3(mdo sde): tham mags pa'i 'bras kyi mtha' gcig kun 'ba'i chos rnams bzhag ste/ rdzing lag pas rgas par zhugs nas kyu khrus mngang nas/ rdzing lan pas rnas pa
115a4(mdo sde): nas byung bshang pan shing a dzu na gang na ba der logs su phrag brkyang ngo // de nas a dzu na'i lal gachen bdud par gyur te/ del bcom ldan 'das kyi
115a5(mdo sde): nas/ dzi lag pas nos pa nas byung ngo // ldeng gyis 'od bsrung ral pa can bsti gnas na 'chag pa na rdzing lag pas nos pa'i 'gras na/ a dzu na'i yal ga chen
115a6(mdo sde): po dung ba zhig mthong ngo // mthong nas kyang 'di snyam du sems te/ a dzu na'i lal chen po 'ding su zhig btung snyam mo// de nas steng rgyas 'od bsrung ral pa
115a7(mdo sde): can bcom ldan 'das gang na ba der song ste byin nas/ bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to// dge sbyong chen po mkhyen par mdzad du gsol/ bdag

115b1(mdo sde): a rdzu na'i yal ga chen po 'di sngon dung par gyur na su zhig gis btud snyam bgyid do// 'od bsrung 'dir bye 'breng nang du yang dag 'jog pa las bzhengs nas rdzing lag

115b3(mdo sde): te/ lus khrus byas nas rdzing lag pas rkos nas byung bar 'dod nas/ shing a rdzu na 'di dag ga na ba de logs su lag pa rkyang ba dang / de nas a rdzu na'i yal ka
115b4(mdo sde): chen po 'di dud par gyur te/ de la ngas 'dzus nas rdzing lag pas rkos nas byung ngo // 'od bsrung 'di ni a rdzu na'i lag pas bzung bar bya'o// de nas lteng rgyas
115b5(mdo sde): 'od srung ral pa can 'di snyam du sems te/ 'di ltar dge sbyong chen po rdzu 'phrul che zhing mthu che ba yin te/ ya mtshan che mod kyi bdag kyang dgra bcom pa ya nin no

115b7(mdo sde): pa'i sha na'i ras gang du bkru snyam mo// de nas lha rnams kyi dbang po brgya byin gyi sems kyis bcom ldan 'das kyi dgongs pa shes pa shes nas/ ri brag gcig
115b8(mdo sde): las rdo leb che la ring ba zhig blangs nas/ bcom ldan 'das gang na ba der song ste phyin nas/ bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan

116a3(mdo sde): lha rnams kyi dbang po brgya byin gyis sems kyis bcom ldan 'das las dgongs pa shes nas/ brag cig las rdo leb che la ring ba zhig khyer nas bcom ldan

117b7(mdo sde): chen po bdag legs par gsungs pa'i chos 'dul ba la rab tu byung ba dang / spen par rdzogs pa dge slong gyi dngos po thob pa lta na/ dge sbyong chen po spyan sngar
